Commentary

A Word of Advice to the Japanese and Koreans Regarding the Wanpaoshan Incident, and Encouragement to Our Fellow Countrymen (Continued) Bin

As mentioned above, we have already understood the true cause of the Wanpaoshan Incident. As for the details of the incident, various domestic newspapers have recently published very detailed accounts, so there is no need for the reporter to repeat them. In order to make it easier for readers to understand the actual situation of the case and the unreasonable atrocities of the Japanese, three tables are listed below:

(1) Table of Land Lease Relationships of Koreans in Wanpaoshan

Location　　　　　　Area of Leased Land　Original Landowners　　　　　　　　　　　　Lessee　　　　　　　　Brief Summary of Contract　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　Sub-Lessee　　　　　　　　Brief Summary of Sub-Lease Contract　　　　　　Remarks

Wanpaoshan　　　500 *xiang*　　　　　　Twelve people including Xiao Hanlin, Zhang Hongbin, and Meng Zhaoye　Hao Yongde, Manager of Changchun Inada Company　Effective for a term of ten years after approval by the Changchun County Government　　　　Nine Koreans including Li Shengxun and Li Zhaohe　　For a term of ten years　　　　　　(1) The lease contract between Hao Yongde and Xiao Hanlin, et al. was not formally approved by Changchun County. (2) Li Shengxun, et al. did not report the lease of the land to the Changchun authorities.

(2) Table of Damages Suffered by Our Farmers Due to the Koreans' Forced Construction of Waterways

Cause　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　Damage　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　Remarks

Koreans digging waterways and diverting water from the Yitong River　Encroachment on farmland along the way, approximately 20 *li* long and 7-8 *zhang* wide　The farmland belongs to 41 other people and has absolutely no contractual relationship with Hao Yongde and Li Shengxun, et al.

The soil excavated from the waterway is piled up on both sides to serve as dikes, approximately 7-8 *zhang* wide and over 20 *li* long　　　Over 400 *mu* of fertile land destroyed in total

The waterway passes through farmland, and the water flow erodes the farmland　　　　(1) The waterway divides each piece of cultivated land into two sections.

For the purpose of irrigating rice paddies, water from the Yitong River is diverted, and water-stopping dams are built across the existing riverbeds, forcing the water into the waterway. The dams obstruct the water flow, causing the river to overflow　(2) The water flow erodes the cultivated land, turning it into wasteland. The low-lying areas on both sides of the upper reaches of the river, over 2,000 *xiang* of farmland are flooded.

The area where Hao Yongde plans to plant rice paddies is relatively high in elevation and has no outlet for drainage　　Hundreds of *xiang* of low-lying farmland in the lower reaches are flooded

The low-lying areas on both sides of the waterway will inevitably be flooded when the river rises　　　Approximately 4-5,000 *xiang*

The Majia Shao Kou of the river is an important passage to and from the west bank. The Koreans are now blocking the water with dams　　　Traffic on both banks is cut off

The Yitong River has always been an important waterway for farmers in Changchun to transport goods during the summer. The Koreans are building dams across the river　　Public transportation is completely cut off

Hundreds of households living along the Yitong River depend on waterway transportation for their livelihood. The Koreans' construction of dams has cut off traffic　　　Livelihoods are all harmed

(3) Table of the Process of Local Negotiations and Japanese Atrocities

Time　　　　　Our Side　　　　　　　　Japanese Side　　　　　　　　　　　　Remarks

June 1st　　　　The Jilin Provincial Government ordered Changchun County to send personnel to cooperate with the county public security police to the dam construction site to persuade the Korean people to stop building the dam and leave the country by peaceful means.　　　The Korean people declared that they would not stop and would not leave the country even if it meant death. The Public Security Bureau took their leaders, Shen, et al., eight people, to the county government. According to their confession, they were ordered by the Japanese to plant rice.

June 3rd　　　　The Changchun County Public Security Bureau Chief and the Guard Team Leader led a team with Shen et al. to Majia Shao Kou where the water ditch was being dug, and physically drove away the Korean people working there.　　　　　Zhou Yuping, the director of the Changchun Municipal Government Preparatory Office, sent a letter to Japanese Consul Tadashi, protesting and demanding investigation of the illegal Korean people, Shen Yongjun et al., who had been detained, as well as the instigators and compensation for our losses.　　　　　After Sino-Japanese consultation, it was agreed to send personnel to investigate the truth on-site and then resolve it fairly. During the investigation period, the Korean people should immediately stop working.

June ?th　　　　　　　　　　　　　The Japanese Consul still ordered the Japanese police to protect the Korean people to continue building the dam.

June 12th　　　The Municipal Government Office sent another letter to the Japanese Consul, stating that the Japanese side should bear full responsibility for any disputes that may arise in the future.

June ?th　　　　　　　　　　　　　The Japanese Consul replied that the dam had not yet started construction, that digging the ditch would not harm farming, and that the dispatched Japanese police were solely responsible for cracking down on the Korean people.

June 17th　　　The Municipal Government Office sent another letter to the Japanese Consul, hoping that both sides would deal with the matter fairly based on the facts investigated.

June ?th　　　The Consul General of Shenyang, Lin, met with Zhang Zuoxiang of the Jilin Provincial Government and made representations. The Provincial Government advocated that the case should still be handled locally and was unwilling to take responsibility, leading to prolonged negotiations. By the end of June, the Korean farmers were intensifying the construction of the dam as the harvest was already delayed. Our farmers, seeing the water overflowing from the paddy fields and encroaching on dry land, and seeing that the autumn harvest was hopeless, were filled with resentment and agreed to drive them away if the Korean people continued to work, and sent representatives to urge the Municipal Government Office to conduct a final negotiation with the Japanese Consul.

June ?th　　　　　　　　　　　　　The Japanese side decided on a policy of "on-site protection" and "promoting dam construction", purchased a large amount of food and transported it to Wanpaoshan, and transported more than 5,000 bundles of willow branches and more than 500 peach soil baskets to supervise the Korean people to speed up the work, requiring completion before July 5th, and forced the Korean people to randomly plant rice seeds on the wasteland of our people, which was everywhere.

June 27th　　　The Municipal Government Office sent another letter to the Japanese Consul to negotiate.

June 30th　　　The farmers and landlords who were harmed in Wanpaoshan Town and the farmers in the nearby rice-growing areas held a rally in Wanpaoshan Town to support resistance to the Koreans' construction of weirs. More than 500 people attended, responsible officers were appointed, and it was decided to fill the trenches and destroy the dikes.

July 2nd　　　　The farmers of Wanpaoshan gathered 400-500 people and implemented the filling of the trenches. The Municipal Government Office sent a letter to the Japanese Consul requesting the withdrawal of the Japanese police and appropriate punishment.　The Japanese police openly fired live ammunition at the farmers, firing a total of 38 shots. The Japanese Consul did not reply to the letter from the Municipal Government Office and sent a garrison and 60 armed police to Wanpaoshan to protect the Korean people's work, surrounding our farmers and the Ma police and strafing them with machine guns, killing more than a dozen farmers and two Ma police officers.　The chief of the Tian Branch of the Third District Police Station under the jurisdiction of Jilin County came forward to mediate and temporarily persuaded the farmers to return.

July 3rd　　　　　　　　　　　　　The Japanese side sent another 16 Japanese police officers, two heavy vehicles, loaded with military tents, military supplies and food, two machine guns, and ammunition, and dug battle trenches in places such as Majia Shao Kou.　Former Japanese Foreign Minister, the Japanese Yen, sent a telegram to the Japanese Consul in Shenyang, stating that the Japanese government, from the point of view of protecting Japanese residents in Manchuria, had to take appropriate measures, and the result might lead to a very serious situation. The Japanese military in Dalian scheduled a combat air defense exercise from the 4th to the 7th, and would demonstrate and publicize along the South Manchurian Railway to Shenyang. 46 Japanese armed police fired 60-70 shots at our suppression police as a demonstration, but no one was injured. The Japanese Consul General in Jilin requested compensation from the Provincial Government for the losses of the Korean farmers.

Note: This table is based on the news reported in various newspapers recently, and there may be errors and omissions.

However, the table can make the reader see the unreasonable atrocities of the Japanese at a glance, so it is presented first and will be revised later.

After the Wanpaoshan Incident occurred, the Japanese still did not realize their errors, as if deeply worried that they would not be able to increase the grief and indignation of our people, increase our people's resentment against Japan, and further incite the Korean people to attack our Korean-based compatriots. According to reports in the continuous newspapers, violent anti-Chinese riots in which Korean mobs brutally massacred our overseas compatriots occurred in Pyongyang, Seoul, Incheon, Jemulpo, Wonsan, Busan, and other cities. There were many deaths, injuries, and losses. The situation is extremely serious. Most of the attacked overseas compatriots fled to Andong, Liaoning, which borders Korea, for refuge. After the purpose of the Korean people's attack had been achieved, they deliberately sent police to suppress them. The Japanese Cabinet also resolved to comfort our overseas compatriots who had been victimized and severely punish the Korean rioters. This kind of deliberately deceptive diplomatic trickery may be considered by the Japanese to be able to cover up the eyes and ears of the people of the world. In fact, their intentions and the truth have long been exposed. The Japanese must defy the great disapproval of the world and repeatedly create unbearable tragedies. What else can we say? To what extent the Wan Incident will expand in the future is difficult to predict at this time. Or it can end here and be shelved as a pending case. It is also possible. But since the Japanese have such determination, there will undoubtedly be more incidents in the coming years that are several times more serious than the Wan Incident. We look at the current situation, mourn the urgency of resisting foreign insults, and grieve for the current hardship of the country. The feeling of grief and indignation is uncontrollable. When I write this, I am truly in tears. Alas, my countrymen, you should also have the same feelings. (To be continued)

Important News

Memorial Meeting of the Central Government and National Government for the Oath-Taking Ceremony

Shao Lizi reports on the process and achievements

Ye Chucang gives a speech on the duties of party members

The Central Party Headquarters held a memorial service at 9:00 a.m. on July 9th for the 5th anniversary of the National Revolutionary Army's Northern Expedition Oath-Taking Ceremony in the auditorium of the Central Party Headquarters. Above the auditorium was a horizontal banner with the four characters "Strive to the End". The slogans on both sides were "Inherit the spirit of the oath-taking ceremony, suppress the traitors, eliminate the Red bandits" and "Guarantee the victory of the Northern Expedition, consolidate unity, and maintain peace." Central Committee members Yu Youren, Shao Lizi, Shao Yuancong, Ye Chucang, Ding Weifen, Chen Lifu, Fang Juehui, Chen BuLei, Wang Boqun, Ke Xinge, Miao Peicheng, and representatives from various agencies and departments, as well as staff members, totaling about five or six hundred people, attended. Ding Weifen presided over the meeting. After the music and ceremony, Shao Lizi reported on the process and achievements of the National Revolutionary Army's Northern Expedition Oath-Taking Ceremony, saying that five years ago today, the National Revolutionary Army held the Northern Expedition Oath-Taking Ceremony in Guangzhou with great enthusiasm. Premier Sun devoted his life to the National Revolution and undertook two Northern Expeditions, which he did not complete.　His will was to carry on to the survivors to inherit their responsibilities and careers. Comrade Chiang Kai-shek was entrusted by the Party to serve as the Commander-in-Chief of the National Revolutionary Army. At that time, with the military and financial resources of Guangdong, he undertook the great cause of the Northern Expedition. The situation was very difficult. Comrade Chiang Kai-shek was determined to follow Premier Sun's will as the standard, carefully observe the trend of popular sentiment, and firmly believe that Guangdong could be unified within one year and the whole country within three years. At that time, Russian advisers on the Northern Expedition military did not advocate advancing from Guangxi and Hunan to the Yangtze River, but advocated following the sea route north from the northern seaports and landing with troops. This was probably for other purposes. Comrade Chiang Kai-shek had the spirit of perseverance and decisively made plans to move forward. At that time, the revolutionary armed forces were far less adequate than the warlords. Relying on all the armed comrades, who believed in the doctrine and received thorough political training, they had strict discipline and uplifted spirit, so they were able to defeat the many with the few. After establishing the capital in Nanjing, they went through many dangers. Sun Chuanfang returned to power and approached the capital area. The Communist Party created disturbances in the rear. The imperialists tried every possible way to destroy them. The National Revolutionary Army moved forward bravely without slackening their fighting spirit due to these obstacles. With one mind, they strove to persevere. In the 17th year, the army arrived in Jinan, and the imperialists colluded with the warlords to obstruct our Northern Expedition, creating the May 3rd Massacre. Comrade Chiang Kai-shek had profound plans and foresaw the location of their poisonous schemes, and would rather endure pain and humiliation than initiate a conflict with them and fall into their trap. With swift military action, he reached Beiping in the shortest time and unified the whole country. Thinking about the pain now, on this memorial occasion, we should remember the difficulty of success and cultivate its spirit. Now, the Communist bandits in the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi are massacring the people in a tragic manner. Commander Chiang Kai-shek, in the midst of the summer heat, is leading his armed comrades in sacrifice and struggle to save the people from fire and water. The National Revolution will not succeed until the Communist bandits are eliminated. What is even more regrettable is that the Japanese deliberately provoked trouble. After the Wanpaoshan Incident occurred, they used the Korean people to massacre our overseas compatriots and implement a strict anti-Chinese policy. Many overseas compatriots were killed, and they wanted to use this opportunity to expand the turmoil and create a second Jinan Massacre, sending troops to the Northeast to achieve their aggressive ambitions. All kinds of conspiracies have been completely exposed. This is truly the autumn of our country's crisis and survival. All my comrades, during this memorial period, should know that the revolution has not yet succeeded, and work together and strive to the end, etc. Shao also proposed that the comrades attending the meeting today observe a moment of silence to express their condolences for the generals who died in the Northern Expedition and the overseas compatriots who were killed by the Korean people this time. Fang Juehui then spoke, saying that the Korean people's anti-Chinese riots this time were a manifestation of the Japanese side's entire plan for China. In the future, we must recognize the Korean people residing in the three northeastern provinces as Japanese residents, not as Korean people, and must correct their names to clarify the responsibility. We must also quickly and accurately investigate the actual number of deaths, injuries, and property losses to provide a basis for negotiations, etc. After the speech, the ceremony ended and the meeting adjourned.

National Government

At 10:00 a.m. on the same day, the National Government held a memorial ceremony for the National Revolutionary Army's Oath-Taking Ceremony. Yu Youren, Shao Lizi, Ye Chucang, Wang Zhengting, Wang Boqun, Ma Fuxiang, Shao Yuancong, Lin Xiang, and representatives from various departments and bureaus, as well as more than two hundred staff members from the National Government's civil service and military affairs offices, attended. Yu Youren presided over the meeting. After leading the ceremony, Ye Chucang gave a speech, saying: Comrades, today we are holding a memorial ceremony for the 5th anniversary of the National Revolutionary Army's Northern Expedition Oath-Taking Ceremony. Five years ago today, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, entrusted by our Party and adhering to Premier Sun's will, launched the Northern Expedition from Guangzhou amidst the warm welcome of the people of the whole country. In the past five years, through constant difficulties and sacrifices, many comrades lost their lives, and at the same time, the people in the war zone have also suffered instability and losses before we have today. In recent years, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has been inspecting and commanding the troops on the front lines during our memorial ceremonies, attacking Feng Yuxiang last year and suppressing the Communists this year. He, along with all the officers and soldiers, has been working hard for the country, regardless of the heat and danger. We should, on the one hand, use boundless enthusiasm to comfort Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and all the officers and soldiers, and on the other hand, cherish Premier Sun's great instructions. At the same time, we should work hard to complete Premier Sun's will in times of difficulty. The armed comrades on the front lines are working hard for the country, and the comrades in the rear should also have their own efforts. However, sometimes we feel that we do not know how to work hard. We think of the comrades on the front lines, who are armed and fighting to save the people. This is the duty of the comrades on the front lines. We should also strive to do our duty. If we can abide by our duty, that is the greatest effort. Often, some people think that it is only possible to be called effort if they bear great responsibilities, do great things, and have high-level plans. If they only abide by their duty, it seems that it is not enough effort. This is a big mistake. I believe that we should only be afraid of not being able to do our duty, and do not worry about not being able to do enough. My comrades should only take one duty, that is, to complete Premier Sun's will. May I ask how much of this great and arduous project has been completed by us in recent years? If we just think about this point, the Party members owe too much and are far from their duty, let alone anything else. Duty is not passive, but active. If we can take the purpose of abiding by our duty, then nothing will be impossible and nothing will be indestructible. Any opinion can be eliminated. I am a local official, and I do not seem to be able to do even one-tenth or one-hundredth of the duty of a local official, so I dare not and should not do anything beyond my duty, because it is already very difficult to complete the duty. A clerk in the government diligently engages in clerical work, and a political official diligently engages in political work. Each performs his duties and does his best, which is to abide by his duty and to strive to do his duty. We should encourage each other to complete Premier Sun's will. Let us think about the people in the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi who are being ravaged by the Red bandits, which has led to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and all the officers and soldiers fighting after the success of the Northern Expedition. At the same time, thinking of the recent heavy rains and disasters, and the harm done by the Communists, who are like floods and fierce beasts, the floods have caused great harm to the local areas, but the local officials have a great responsibility for disaster relief and preparedness. Now, let me ask how much has been done? In view of the efforts of the officers and soldiers on the front lines, the comrades in the rear should encourage each other more carefully. If we can abide by our duties, so that the war against the Red bandits can end soon and the construction undertakings can be completed as soon as possible, on this memorial day, comrades should recall the difficulties of the past and work harder to achieve the ideal and hope of political affairs as soon as possible. Everyone must encourage each other to work hard in order to be worthy of the officers and soldiers who died since the Northern Expedition and Premier Sun's instructions to us.

The Truth About the Japanese Police Atrocities in the Wanpaoshan Incident

More than a dozen Chinese wounded, two or three dead, and more than a dozen arrested

The Japanese army stationed in Changchun urgently decided to mobilize on a large scale

Various Chinese organizations in Changchun also decided on countermeasures

Taking the withdrawal of Japanese troops and the release of Chinese farmers as a prerequisite

Changchun dispatch: The Sino-Japanese rice paddy negotiations in Wanpaoshan are worsening. The local landlords and villagers who have been harmed, seeing that the government is unable to drive away the Korean people and stop the digging work, have to take self-defense actions. Therefore, the support association has gathered four or five hundred farmers and workers, each holding shovels and hoes, and started filling the trenches at 7:38 a.m. on the 2nd of this month. Unexpectedly, a dozen Japanese police officers protecting the rice paddies opened fire. The smoke filled the sky. Dozens of Chinese farmers were injured, and two or three died. After the Chinese people retreated into the village courtyard, the Japanese police continued to pursue them and arrested fifteen or sixteen villagers, severely torturing them with hanging, pouring kerosene and chili water, and flogging them with clubs. They were covered with scars. Then they were transferred from Wanpaoshan to the Japanese police station for detention. After the tragedy occurred, the Japanese police department sent out carrier pigeons to report to the Japanese consulate and police station in Changchun. Consul Tadashi and Police Chief Take Nami reported the incident. At 11:48 a.m. on the 2nd, they dispatched three teams of ten Japanese police officers in two military vehicles, fully loaded with guns and ammunition, to provide assistance and issued orders for appropriate action. This group of Japanese police officers arrived at Wanpaoshan Town at 2:55 p.m. and rushed to the rice paddies to assist the Japanese police, going to various villages to continue arresting people and confiscating self-defense guns and ammunition from Chinese farmers. At the same time, Japanese Consul Tadashi and Police Chief Takenami gathered the 3rd Brigade, the 4th Regiment, and the Gendarmerie at the consulate for an emergency military meeting. Commander Nakagawakinzo and Squadron Leader Major Nakamura and others attended, totaling fifty or sixty people. The meeting resulted in five resolutions: (1) continue to send troops and take decisive measures, using maximum force to suppress the Chinese farmers; (2) issue an ultimatum to the Chinese government, demanding a satisfactory reply within 48 hours, otherwise, take final action; (3) Japan will provide practical assistance to the Korean people in the Wanpaoshan rice paddies and continue to urge them to work; (4) call for assistance from all Japanese people in Manchuria and assist in publicity in public opinion; (5) send telegrams to the Japanese government, the Lushun Civil Administration Office, the Kanto Office, and the highest Chinese government officials regarding the rice paddy case and the current situation, and lodge serious protests. In addition, a mobilization order was issued and troops were dispatched. It was found that around 3:00 p.m. on the 2nd, 50 cavalrymen from the garrison set off from Changchun. At 11:20 a.m. on the 3rd, another 20 military policemen were sent to provide assistance. Around 1:00 p.m., another 500 police officers were dispatched, all equipped with two machine guns, two rapid-fire cannons, five or six boxes of ammunition, five hundred artillery shells, and more than two hundred large guns, hundreds of small guns, and more than 10,000 rounds of ammunition. They were issued to the Korean people for "self-defense", but in reality, they were preparing for war. By 2:00 p.m. on the 3rd, a large number of Japanese police and troops had left Changchun one after another and went straight to Wanpaoshan.

Our government authorities are still dealing with this kind of Japanese atrocity calmly. In addition to immediately notifying the county government and public security bureau by telegram from the Third Public Security Branch of the county district to request instructions, the county government reported to the municipal government office and the foreign affairs department, requesting that a protest be lodged with Japan immediately to avoid expanding the scope of the negotiations. The municipal director and foreign affairs director, Zhou Yuping, considered that the Japanese police had opened fire on unarmed farmers, which was inhumane and damaging to national relations. Furthermore, the large-scale dispatch of troops to demonstrate and suppress was a breach of agreement. On the 2nd and 3rd, he summoned County Magistrate Ma, Chamber of Commerce President Sun, Public Security Bureau Chief Lu, Security Team Chief Tang, and leaders of local organizations to the office for an emergency meeting. As a result, it was decided (1) to lodge a final protest with Japan, requesting the withdrawal of the dispatched military police and to stop their illegal activities; (2) the county government would quickly dispatch 300 police and security forces to protect the farmers and monitor the actions of the Japanese army; (3) send personnel to investigate the cause of the disturbance and to express condolences to the wounded and dead villagers; (4) instruct the Japanese consul to order the Korean people to stop digging trenches and building dams and to await resolution by the Sino-Japanese governments; (5) report the truth about the Japanese police firing on our farmers by telegram to the Liaoning and Jilin provincial governments and to the Japanese consul general for serious negotiations; (6) the foreign affairs department requested the Japanese consul to release all the more than ten arrested Chinese people and to compensate our wounded and dead. Based on the above countermeasures, in addition to handling the matter, Director Zhou personally went to the Japanese consulate in Changchun on the 2nd and 3rd and had face-to-face negotiations with Tadashi Judoku, demanding the withdrawal of a large number of military police and the release of the arrested Chinese farmers as a prerequisite, and other matters would be negotiated later. However, after the tragedy occurred, the citizens were very angry and organized a diplomatic support association to serve as a backing for the government and to provide practical assistance to the negotiations, which is currently being actively prepared and will be realized in the near future (July 3rd).

Overseas Chinese in Korea Arrive in Beijing to Plead

Korean People Gathered in Mobs and Tragically Harmed Overseas Chinese

Earnestly Requesting the Government and Yuan to Lodge Serious Protests with Japan

Beijing News: The tragic case of Korean people massacring Chinese people, which has caused a national sensation, has aroused the public outrage in all circles of our country. The Incheon Chinese Chamber of Commerce in Korea, due to Korean people gathering in mobs and tragically injuring our overseas compatriots, and the lives and property of the overseas compatriots are in imminent danger, yesterday dispatched representatives Liu Zhongkui and Cao Jingyu, who rushed to Beijing overnight, carrying petitions, earnestly asking the National Government, the Central Party Headquarters, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee to care about the lives of the people, pay attention to the commercial situation, and quickly negotiate seriously with the Japanese envoy, and to urgently telegraph the Governor-General of Korea to quickly stop the atrocities of the Korean people and find ways to protect the lives and property of the Chinese people in order to save overseas Chinese merchants and maintain the industry. The original text of the representatives' petitions to the National Government and various Yuan and ministries is recorded below and published separately.

Submission to the National Government Original Text

Respectfully submitted regarding the violent uprising of Koreans, the tragic injury to the property and lives of overseas Chinese, the escalating situation, and the urgent need to request the swift issuance of an order to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to devise a means of stopping it, in order to protect overseas Chinese property and preserve the lives of our people. It is our understanding that the initial cause of the conflict between Chinese and Korean farmers in Wanbaoshan, Jilin, was the unreasonable and overbearing behavior of the Korean people. However, Japanese newspapers openly fabricated stories of Chinese people oppressing Koreans, deliberately stirring up trouble and exaggerating the situation to incite the gullible Korean population, creating animosity between the two sides. Their country seeks to use the hands of the Koreans to achieve its goal of expelling our overseas Chinese. The Korean people, without examining the facts or considering justice, relied solely on one-sided accounts, recklessly indulging in their cruel intentions. Like a gathering storm, they expanded their actions together. Recently, in places such as the capital, Incheon, Wonsan, Busan, and Pyongyang, tragedies of murdering Chinese people similar to those in 1927 have unfolded, surpassing them in severity. Like a wildfire, they cannot be approached. Detailed information has been published in various newspapers in recent days. Merchants have also received numerous urgent telegrams. Countless Chinese merchants in Korea have been forced to suspend their businesses, their property and lives destroyed. The perilous situation worsens with each passing day. Upon investigation, it is found that the areas of the capital, Incheon, Wonsan, Busan, and Pyongyang are all prosperous and important regions of Korea, heavily guarded by military police. Yet, such events have occurred openly. What more can be said of remote areas? If swift action is not taken to stop it, it will inevitably spread throughout Korea. It is clear that the property and lives of hundreds of thousands of overseas Chinese merchants in Korea are at risk, and the cruelty will undoubtedly lead to unimaginable consequences. At this critical moment of survival, we are compelled to represent all overseas Chinese merchants in Korea and appeal to you urgently, requesting your government to immediately order the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to lodge a serious protest with the Japanese ambassador, and to request the ambassador to urgently telegraph the Governor-General of Korea to quickly stop the violent actions of the Koreans and to take full responsibility for protecting the safety of the lives and property of our overseas Chinese. As for the punishment of the perpetrators and compensation, we ask that you first declare and reserve the right to address these matters later. We submit this urgent appeal with utmost concern and anxiety to Chiang, Chairman of the National Government.

Submission to the Executive Yuan

Respectfully submitted regarding the violent uprising of Koreans, the tragic injury to overseas Chinese, the escalating situation, and the urgent need to request the swift transfer to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to devise a means of stopping it, in order to protect overseas Chinese property and preserve lives. It is our understanding that the initial cause of the conflict between Chinese and Korean farmers in Wanbaoshan, Jilin, was the unreasonable and overbearing behavior of the Korean people. However, the media in that country fabricated stories of Chinese people oppressing Koreans, deliberately inciting emotions and exaggerating the situation to sensationalize it. The farmers of that country also failed to examine the facts or investigate justice, relying solely on the clamor of the media, recklessly indulging in their cruel and violent intentions. Like a gathering storm, they blindly followed and joined in. Recently, in places such as the capital, Incheon, Wonsan, and Busan, tragedies of hating and murdering Chinese people similar to those in 1927 have unfolded. Detailed information has been published in the Shen Bao and Xin Bao newspapers on July 5th and 6th. Merchants have also received numerous telegrams, and countless businesses have been forced to suspend operations. The situation is becoming increasingly dangerous, and the situation is precarious. Upon investigation, it is found that the areas of the capital, Incheon, Busan, and Wonsan are all major regions of Korea, heavily guarded by military police. Yet, such events have occurred. Remote areas must be even worse. If swift action is not taken to stop it, it will inevitably spread throughout Korea, leading to unimaginable consequences. It is clear that the lives and property of tens of thousands of overseas Chinese merchants in Korea are in imminent danger of complete ruin, with no way to protect themselves. The cruel situation could not be worse. At this critical moment of life and death, we are compelled to send representatives Liu Zhongkui and Zeng Jingyu overnight to appeal to you urgently, requesting your government to immediately transfer this matter to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, to immediately notify the Japanese Consulate, and to urgently telegraph the Governor-General of Korea to quickly stop the violent actions of the Koreans and devise a means of protecting the safety of the overseas Chinese. We submit this urgent appeal with utmost anxiety and await your orders to the President of the Executive Yuan.

Circumstances of Sino-Russian Talks

Mr. Wu Run, Secretary of the Delegation, Returns Home

The Issue of Redeeming the Railway is Changed to Informal Discussions Outside of the Meeting

Harbin Dispatch: Regarding the progress of discussions in the Sino-Russian talks on the issue of redeeming the railway, the lack of detailed reports from Mo Dehui upon his return home has left the nation uncertain about the specifics. Yesterday at 8:00 AM, Mr. Wu Run, secretary of the delegation, and Ms. Fu Dejin, clerk, returned home together. I visited Mr. Wu at the Beijing Hotel at 9:30 PM last night and inquired about the progress of the meeting. According to him, his return home was to deliver diplomatic documents, which have already been submitted to the Office of the Superintendent of the Eastern Railway and forwarded to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Tomorrow, he will go to Liaoning to visit his family and, if necessary, go to Beiping to meet with the Deputy Commander to report. The round trip will take three weeks, and he will return to Russia via this route. The two special envoys, Tu Wei Zeng and Wang Zeng'en, who returned home earlier, have been urged by Mo Quan to return quickly. It is estimated that the two gentlemen will depart for Russia around July 10th. Since Mo Quan's second trip to Russia, the Sino-Russian talks have held six formal meetings on the issue of redeeming the railway and three meetings on changing the Eastern Railway's management methods. Since the ninth meeting, the intervals between formal sessions have gradually shortened. The ninth meeting was held on June 21st, the tenth on June 24th, and the eleventh on June 29th. The twelfth meeting is scheduled for July 4th. Both parties are unwilling to prolong the meeting period, so progress has been quite active. Due to the vastness of the railway's assets, including locomotives, bridges, tracks, and culverts, it is difficult to estimate the price without specialized technical personnel. However, this cannot be accomplished in a short period of time. Both parties agreed to change the issue to informal discussions outside of the meeting to save time. The two plenipotentiaries will hold informal discussions, and they are currently discussing the procedures to expedite the case and how to negotiate the price. Therefore, there has been no actual standstill. Previous reports in domestic and foreign newspapers claiming that Russia had demanded 1.8 billion were premature because neither party is currently prepared to demand or offer a price. The Chinese side proposed the issue of changing the Eastern Railway's management methods because there are many outstanding issues with the Eastern Railway that the Council has not resolved over the years. Therefore, it was specifically raised for discussion at this time. Both parties are currently studying the agenda, and it has not yet reached the stage of formally discussing counter-proposals. It is difficult to predict Russia's views on redeeming the railway and changing the railway's management methods. However, the diplomatic situation changes depending on the political situation in both countries. Recently, the Russian side has observed slight fluctuations in our country's political situation and inevitably harbors a wait-and-see attitude towards the meeting. Recent Japanese newspaper reports claiming that Britain and Russia have proposed twelve management method proposals and that we have proposed eight are purely fabricated. It is hoped that domestic newspapers will correct this. Mo Quan has no intention of returning home to report. The spreading of this rumor is also propagated by a third party and contains ulterior motives. (July 4th)

Fang and Shao's Factions Attempt to Flee to Wuyuan

Unable to Enter Fujian, Bandit Gangs Plan to Invade Anhui

Currently Encircled and About to be Eliminated

Wuyuan Dispatch: The two bandit factions of Fang Zhimin and Shao Shiping in Eastern Jiangxi, after being besieged by the Ruan and Xu divisions in March, fled from Guangfeng and Qianshan to the areas of Pucheng, Chong'an, Shangxia Mei in Northern Fujian, colluding with local Triad members, engaging in rampant arson and looting. Subsequently, the Fujian provincial defense forces, Qian Yuguang's brigade, the marine corps of Lin Bingzhou's brigade, and the units of Zhou Zequn and Liu Shangzhi, advanced in separate routes to suppress them. The Fang faction then withdrew from Fujian and fled back to Tai'an in Jiangxi Province. Recently, due to Jiangxi Province's large-scale suppression of the Communists, the Ruan division stationed in Eastern Jiangxi also actively encircled the Fang and Shao bandit factions. They made contact with the main force of the Fang and Shao factions in Wannian. The Fang bandits were unable to withstand the attack, suffering a major defeat and collapse. Their remaining two thousand or so men, led by Shao Shiping, fled from Wannian to the eight or nine districts of Dexing, and then planned to directly attack Wucheng (the eight districts are forty miles from Wucheng), hoping to resist stubbornly by relying on the terrain. On the 27th of last month, the Shao faction crossed the river at Tongbu and invaded the southern territory of Wuyuan. At 6:00 AM that day, they captured Caomen Village, looting all of its hundred or so households. At 9:00 AM, another large force of five or six hundred men attacked Taibai Town. The local self-defense corps of the town initially resisted fiercely, but later retreated due to being outnumbered. The bandits then entered the market and searched, sparing no business in the entire town. Before leaving, they kidnapped four hostages, including the grandson of tea merchant Xue Yucheng, demanding a ransom of 4,000 yuan, giving them three days to prepare the money and bring it to Wang Village in Shitian for redemption, or they would tear up the tickets. Nearby Dong Village and six or seven other villages were all searched and looted. After their plunder, they returned to the eight districts of Dexing. On the same day, a tea boat from northern Wuyuan was passing through Tongbu when it was spotted by the bandits, who opened fire to stop it. All the hundreds of cases of tea on the boat were moved ashore. The four members of the boat's crew, Jin Xinyan and his father, were also kidnapped, demanding a ransom of 10,000 yuan. It is reported that the cases of tea carried on this boat were all famous Chouxin Zhenmei teas from northern Wuyuan, worth a huge sum of money. For a time, the situation on the border of Wuyuan became very tense. Magistrate Gao received an alarm about the capture of Taibai and Caomen, and considering the weakness of the city's defenses, he consulted with Zhang's Deputy Battalion Commander of the 55th Division's guerrilla forces and dispatched dozens of soldiers, together with the county police brigade and the Wuyuan southern militia, to pursue them. Because the bandits did not advance, on the 28th, the bandits became even more rampant. The main force of Shao's bandits actually attempted to enter the entire city of Wucheng. Zhang's Deputy Battalion Commander, realizing the perilous situation, immediately ordered martial law. He first closed the city gates on the northeast, south, and east sides, leaving only the west gate open. The ferry across the river surrounding the city was closed, and land and water traffic was cut off, prohibiting people from freely entering or leaving. He also prohibited moving goods or relocating. On one side, the houses near the city walls were demolished, and on the other, the villagers were recruited, with each family sending one person, each holding a bird gun or hunting gun, along with the merchant corps and police team, to climb the city walls and defend them in strict formation. On the 29th and 30th, the military and civilians patrolled the city, not slacking off for two nights. The villages in the Zhongyun area of the southern countryside, fearing that the bandits would attack the county seat, which was an inevitable route, also summoned three thousand hunters and farmers from various districts, each holding a flintlock, pine cannon, and concentrated them at Baishi Cen, a strategic pass leading from Jiangxi, to block and intercept them. Therefore, Shao's bandits retreated from Haikou to Nuanshui Jiudu Jiaocun yesterday (30th). Today, the city defenses have not been lifted because the bandits have not retreated far. However, according to a report from Zhongyun this afternoon, a battalion of reinforcements has arrived in Taibai, and part of the Fourth Division is also being deployed from Yushan to Wuyuan. Two regiments of the 55th Division continued to arrive in Dexing, and Division Commander Ruan also personally arrived in Deyi to command. People's hearts were slightly comforted. Moreover, Shao's bandits are already surrounded. Once the various armies launch a joint attack, it will not be difficult to eliminate them in one fell swoop. (July 1st)

The Catastrophe of Flooding in Northwest Jiang of Guangdong Province

More than 40,000 Refugees in North River, with More Than 10,000 Drowned and Starved to Death

Dozens of Enclosures Collapsed in Various Places, the Tragedy No Less Than in the Year of Yimao

Guangzhou Dispatch: The floods in the Northwest River this time have been disastrous. The West River basin has become a swamp. The disaster situation in the North River is no less than in the year of Yimao. Taking only the disaster areas in the Yingde, Qingyuan, and Yuantan areas as an example, there are currently more than 40,000 refugees in the disaster area. About four or five thousand people have drowned or starved to death. The property loss is no less than several million yuan. The disaster situation in various places obtained in recent days is recorded separately as follows:

North River

Along the Guangshao Road to the villages near Yuantan Station, no roof ridge can be seen. The entire area is a vast expanse of water. The water in the rice fields is more than twenty feet deep. Refugees are scattered on the hills, exposed to the wind and eating in the open. In Fuan Village, District Eight of Qingyuan, the floodwaters are more than thirty feet deep. About 5,000 refugees are there. Seeing the Guangzhou relief team arrive, they rushed to them in small boats, dividing the food among themselves. These refugees have not eaten for several days. According to the investigation of the relief team, there are currently more than 6,000 refugees in Zhouxin Township, Qingyuan, about 3,000 disaster victims in Dalangdi Township, about 2,000 disaster victims in Dayou Liao Township, about 6,000 at the mouth of the Pijiang River, about 4,000 refugees in Hengshi, about 3,000 refugees in Lidong, and refugees in smaller and more remote villages are too numerous to count. About two-thirds of the houses in each village have collapsed, and the rice fields and fruit trees have been completely washed away. No less than two or thirty of the levees in each village have been breached. Among them, the Shijiao Levee in Qingyuan is the most important because the levee is at the key point where the northern flood goes south. It was on the verge of collapsing twice this time. Fortunately, the villagers nearby knew the relationship with their lives and property. In advance, all the men were conscripted to guard the levee. On the first of this month, the levee was breached by the floodwaters of the North River by seven or eight feet. The villagers immediately sounded the alarm to rescue and gathered thousands of people to transport pre-stored sandbags to block the breach, which turned the crisis into safety. Extending to 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 3rd, it suddenly rained heavily, and mountain floods broke out again. The water flow was more rapid than before. The Shijiao Levee was breached again by two or three feet. The villagers rescued at the risk of their lives, and seven or eight sand-carrying boats filled the breach, and dozens of villages inside the levee were spared from disaster. However, the floodwaters flooded all the villages, and it has been more than three feet deep. On the night of the 3rd, Dalang Yue was breached by several feet. From Yuantan and below, although the water level has been slower since the 4th, it is still a vast expanse of water. Currently, the loss to the Yue Shao Railway is about 300,000 to 400,000 yuan because the subgrade above and below Pijiang Station has collapsed for a total of more than 600 feet. More than a thousand feet of the 61st pile position of Shao Station has collapsed, and another 2,000 feet have collapsed in Bancun. The full road will not be repaired and opened to traffic in less than a month's project.

West River

Among the disaster areas in the West River, the area under the jurisdiction of Sanshui County is the most tragic because the southwest of Sanshui is the confluence of the West River and the North River into the Pearl River. From Huangtang along Mafang, about twenty miles below Luba in Sanshui, to Hekou, Shiwanshan and Foshan, the two banks have become swamps. The rice fields have been submerged. At 3:00 AM one morning, the Daqiang Levee near Shangtang (this levee is a barrier for the Shijiao Levee in Qingyuan) collapsed for several hundred feet. Various places inside the levee have become huge immersions. Also, the Meitai Levee in the northern district of Sanshui also collapsed by more than a hundred feet. This levee was breached once in the flood in the year of Yimao. This is the second collapse. Only one-third of the disaster victims in nearby villages escaped. Also, the Mumian base levee under the county's jurisdiction suddenly broke through at 3:00 AM on the night of the 30th of last month. Fortunately, the rescue was effective and did not cause a horizontal break. However, it was in danger again on the evening of the 1st of this month. The villagers rescued day and night and managed to support it. As for the Dapu Levee, it was ineffective to rescue it, and finally dozens of feet of breaches. The water was terrible, and more than a dozen villages became swamps. The Xiebian Levee under the jurisdiction of Nanhai has been breached and blocked repeatedly in recent days. The southwest station of the Guangsan Road has been submerged by water. Passengers use boats instead of walking. Along the Guangsan Railway subgrade, it is also in a huge immersion. The rails of the Sanyanqiao, Tanbian, Chatou Henghe and five stations have been flooded by West flood. (July 7th and 5th)

Unprecedented Flood in Eastern Anhui

Mingguang Dispatch: In the areas of Gan Ding in Eastern Anhui, there has been heavy rain for days, causing mountain torrents and a sudden rise in river water of seventeen or eight feet. Dozens of villages on both sides have been submerged, and countless people have died. Mingbu, Hexia, Hexi and other streets are a vast expanse of water. It has become a swamp. More than 4,000 houses have been flooded and destroyed. The grain and miscellaneous objects have been completely swept away. The loss is estimated to be more than 300,000 yuan. This is truly an unprecedented robbery. The water this time was turbulent and abnormal. It only rose four or five feet deep at first, but at about 3:00 AM on the 6th, it suddenly surged, rushing and surging. The water was terrible. Within three or four hours, it rose more than a foot again, so most of the residents in low-lying areas did not have time to avoid it, and some were tragically drowned in their sleep. The Mingnan Railway has been flooded. The Railway Bureau has sent engineering personnel to inspect it. The second express train opened to Tianjin that day was blocked at Xiaobian Village and did not arrive at Ming Station until after 5:00. (July 7th)

Songjiang

Department Order Prohibiting Stone Quarrying in Tianma Mountain

It is now known that the Ministry of Finance has ordered the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance to do so and has also informed the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mines to revoke the departmental certificate and prohibit mining. The Financial Department also instructed the Shatianshan official property affairs bureau to strictly implement it. The Financial Department's order is recorded as follows: It is ordered to comply with the matter. The instructions of the Ministry of Finance, No. 43776, are hereby presented. This department is presented to report on the situation of Jiang Erchang's report on Tianma Mountain, which is to be transferred for verification and ordered to be followed. The details are as follows: It is known that Jiang and Chang's report on Tianma Mountain's official mountain is for the purpose of donating to the Party Department to build public houses and preserve tombs. It was also ordered by the former Jiangsu Shatian official property affairs bureau that stone quarrying should not be carried out. Jiang Erchang and his wife Jiang Jinheying were not allowed to rent it out to stone merchants for stone quarrying and grave digging, and they encroached on more than 30 acres of official wasteland. It is not appropriate to do so. The departmental certificate should be revoked immediately and the Agricultural and Mining Department should be notified to cancel the registration and prohibit stone quarrying. The Third Interrogation Record of Li Leng's Bribery Case

The local court opened the third investigation court yesterday (9th) at 11:00 AM on the case of Li Leng, the former county magistrate of Jiangyin, Yang Ying, the former auditor, and Li Zonggang, the former director of the Public Security Bureau, who were accused of accepting bribes for opium. Li Zonggang, Yang Ying, and Li Pinxian, a person involved, were reported to have reported to the court. Zhao Jieshou and Qian Yaojiang of Chen Qing Bao reported that they had arrived. Li Zhibin, Meng Fushou, Lin Fengxiang, Chen Yifeng, and Hu Ayu, the former section chiefs of the Public Security Bureau's third section, were not available for detention. After interrogating them by Prosecutor Lu, regarding Qian Yaojiang, he was asked who contacted him when Chen Qing Bao published on January 26 that someone had bribed 30 yuan in the local case. Qian claimed that Wu Shanbao refused to contact him. Chen Qing Bao published an article on June 19 about Qian Zuopeng's smoke case, saying that there were 4,000 yuan in bribes. Zhao said that he was not in the museum, but the news had been corrected on the 23rd, considering it inaccurate. Li Zonggang asked where the archives of Qian Zuopeng's family smoke case were. Wuxi

Jiangsu Province Business Tax Regional Collection

The Jiangsu Province business tax, since the provincial government ordered its collection by individual counties, has seen business tax bureau chiefs from each county meeting with chambers of commerce and various industries to discuss implementation. However, as this is a new tax, its implementation has been extremely difficult. For months, much effort has been expended. Currently, in various counties south of the Yangtze River, such as Zhenjiang, Wuxi, Wuxian, Wujin, Jiangyin, Changshu, Liyang, Yixing, etc., arrangements are mostly in place, and the amounts to be paid have also been determined. Recently, the newly appointed Finance Commissioner Xu Baoying, considering that the tax amounts have already been individually agreed upon by various industries, simplifying bureau affairs, decided to implement a regional approach for improved coordination and cost savings. Several counties will be grouped into one region. Those already determined include Wuxi, Changshu, Jiangyin, and Liyang as one region, establishing a regional business tax bureau with its office in Wuxi, and Yang Wobian as the bureau chief. Additionally, Wuxian, Wujiang, Kunshan, and Taicang form another region, with the bureau located in Wuxian, and Wang Shutang as the bureau chief. In the abolished counties, a tax supervisor will be appointed to handle business tax matters in that county, under the control of the regional business tax bureau. This has been formally announced and is to be implemented immediately.

A Shocking City Robbery

In Daliu Lane, behind the Qin family residence in this county, there is a doctor named Wang Dao'an, over fifty years old, originally from Yancheng, who has been in Wuxi for nineteen years. He married a woman named Zhang, and they have a son and a daughter, named Aiqing and Lanying, respectively. Aiqing is already married. The family of four lived in harmony. Yesterday (the 9th), at five o'clock in the morning, four robbers suddenly arrived, each holding a Browning pistol. Three robbers entered the house while one kept watch outside. After entering, they claimed, "Is Dr. Wang at home? We have come specifically to ask him to see a patient." Thereupon, his daughter Lanying replied that her father was in his room. Upon hearing this, the robbers went straight into the room. At that moment, Wang Dao'an, seeing the situation, knew they were robbers and immediately got out of bed, intending to escape. However, he was seized by the robbers, who forcibly removed the two gold rings he was wearing. They then searched the bed and took a leather suitcase containing a pawn ticket and thirty-eight silver dollars. Not satisfied, the robbers tied up his daughter Lanying with rope, forcing her to reveal the location of the hidden silver. Lanying replied that it was in the room, and the robbers then re-entered the room, overturning boxes and chests, and looting extensively. In total, they stole three hundred and fifty silver dollars in banknotes, thirty silver dollars in cash, two hundred and fifty dimes, and a leather coat, valued at over seven hundred dollars. After obtaining the loot, the robbers carried it out the door and tightly fastened the bolt on the Wang family's gate with lead wire, preventing the residents from going outside to report the incident.

Zhenjiang

Merchants and Residents Appeal Against Demolition

Over one hundred merchant and resident households outside Zhenjiang's West Gate, along the canal, have been ordered by the Provincial Capital Construction Project Office to demolish their houses by the 20th of this month, which poses significant difficulties. Therefore, they have specifically petitioned the Chamber of Commerce to advocate on their behalf.

Head of Provincial Hospital Released on Bail

Dr. Wang Yuanchen, the head of the Provincial Hospital, was sued in the Criminal Court of the Zhenjiang District Court by a man named Yi for professional negligence causing disability. During an operation to treat Yi's external injury, Wang allegedly reattached Yi's leg bone incorrectly, rendering Yi immobile and beyond further medical treatment. After being summoned by the court, Wang Yuanchen appeared for questioning at 10 a.m. yesterday, along with witnesses Zhao Zisheng and Liu Yusheng. The plaintiff, Yi, was unable to attend due to his mobility issues. The witnesses were questioned first, followed by the defendant, Wang Yuanchen. Wang stated that because the hospital's equipment was incomplete, he had Yi taken to the Hongren Hospital for X-ray examination, where it was discovered that the bone had been broken. He then performed surgery to fix it, but because it was too painful, he sent Yi back to Hongren to be checked with gas. It was then discovered that the bone had been reattached incorrectly. Wang added that mistakes had been made before, and that his treatment of Yi, twisting the leg and reattaching the bone, was merely an experiment. The questioning of the witnesses continued. After the questioning, Wang Yuanchen was ordered to be released on bail, and the court adjourned.

Lawsuit Regarding a Passenger's Body Thrown into the River

The Dada Company's Dahe Steamer, while operating the Yangzhou-Shanghai route the day before yesterday, mistakenly threw passenger Mr. Jia's body into the river near Tiansheng Port. This was reported by the Nantong County Government, which ordered the head of the local Public Security Bureau, Director Tang, to investigate thoroughly. However, the reply was ambiguous and suspected of bribery, leading to another report. The local court recused itself according to law. The case files have been transferred for review, and summonses will be issued to the parties involved for investigation according to the law.

It emerged from the water, only to be swept eastwards by the waves. Residents alerted the neighborhood watch and attempted to retrieve it, but it was already beyond reach. Continuous Rain Causes Disaster and Flooding of Enclosed Fields

County Magistrate Peng Interrogates the Hongwan Case

In April of last year, the former county magistrate, Li Leng, upon assuming office, was ordered to secretly investigate the Hongwan case at Zhangqing Gate, involving the former head of the detective team, Huang Bingzhong. The case remained unresolved for a year. Huang Bingzhong has now voluntarily turned himself in. Huang Bingzhong also vehemently denied any involvement. After the interrogation, it was decided that Jiang Weisheng would be summoned for questioning next time. Huang Bingzhong and others were released on bail.

Nantong

Major Flood in Eastern Township Leads to Incident

In the eastern townships of Nantong, including Yiyu, Jinsha, Shigang, and Qian'an, which are historically salt production areas and have lower terrain, shaped like the bottom of a pot, a major flood has occurred. The upstream areas clashed with the downstream Sanyu area due to the opening of dams. The Sanyu Self-Defense Corps opened fire, killing several villagers from Dongshe Township, provoking outrage from the upstream areas. On the 8th, they mobilized their self-defense corps to head there. Upon learning of this, the county government immediately sent a telegram to stop them. County Magistrate Zhang and the Construction Bureau technician Zhang Ruhong rushed to mediate.

Martial Law Declared in Bandit-Infested Area at the Border of Tongzhou and Rugao

In areas bordering Tongzhou and Rugao, such as Zhantao and Jiuhua Mountain, bandits have been causing disturbances. The ringleader, Zhu Daoshi, also known as Hunkian Hou, and five others have been captured and sent to the Rugao County Government for interrogation. Due to the continued bandit activity, the police and local militia have declared temporary martial law.

Delineated Area of Opium Suppression in Tongzhou

Zhu Jun, the Director of the Tongzhou Opium Suppression Bureau, had only just settled the area of jurisdiction. He was also assigned to concurrently administer Rugao, Haimen, Qidong, and Chongming, each with a sub-bureau. The former Special Commissioner for the Inspection of Special Goods Sales has been abolished and merged into the Opium Suppression Bureau. The provincial bureau will assign someone else to handle tax collection. A company of the Protection and Arrest Team has been assigned from the Nantong area and is expected to arrive within days.

Jiaxing

Thorough Investigation of Opium Case by the Third District Office

Pan Qinghua, the District Chief of the Third District Office in Wangjiangjing, Jiaxing, searched the Wancheng Rice Shop for opium a few days ago, causing a strike among the rice merchants in the town. The county chamber of commerce petitioned the county government to send someone to investigate and stabilize the business community. It is now known that the merchants and residents of the town are outraged by this incident and have jointly submitted a petition to the province from over thirty businesses, accusing Pan of illegal actions. Pan also knows that he cannot remain in his position and has submitted his resignation. The county government sent someone to Wangjiangjing on the 8th to investigate everything and submit a report to the provincial government for review.

Huzhou

Hengtong Pawnshop Clerk Drowns in Capsized Boat

The Hengtong Pawnshop in Hongxingqiao is a branch of the Hengyu Pawnshop on Guanhua River in this city. In recent years, due to the presence of many bandits in the western townships, the pawnshop transfers valuable jewelry to pawnshops in Huzhou. Hengtong sends clerks to Huzhou to transport these items, using their own long boat every few days. On the 5th of this month, Hengtong sent clerks Liang Dacai and Chen Shoubao to Huzhou to retrieve goods by boat. The next morning, they took five hundred silver dollars and a package of jewelry. Liang, Chen, and the boatmen returned to Hongxingqiao on the same boat. While passing by the Dade Bridge, about three miles from Hongxingqiao, the boatman was careless and capsized the boat. Chen and the boatmen managed to swim to safety, but Liang Dacai tragically drowned. The pawnshops in Huzhou and Hongxingqiao hired many local boats to search the area where the incident occurred, but his body has not yet been found. It is reported that the deceased was from Hang County, and the pawnshop has notified his family by telegram.

Textile Industry Unrest Remains Unresolved

The Dingxin Textile Shop on North Street in this city held a sales promotion after its opening, but failed to discard the expired advertising materials. They were questioned by other businesses, leading to a physical altercation in which Dingxin's cabinet was overturned and Zhan Dafu, an employee of the Tongyu Shop, was injured in the nose. Afterwards, the city Chamber of Commerce convened a meeting of textile industry peers to discuss the matter. As a result, it was resolved that (1) closing the market would harm both parties, so business should resume as usual; (2) all industries are permanently prohibited from holding promotions that disrupt the market unless approved by the relevant industry association, and the county government should issue a notice prohibiting such promotions; (3) as a form of punishment for Dingxin, Dingxin should provide a certain amount of compensation to the industry association's welfare fund. The perpetrators, Ding and Zhang, and the Dingxin manager, Cheng Xiaoyun, would jointly publish an apology to their peers and request the withdrawal of the lawsuit, with Dingxin providing medical expenses to the injured party. After the resolutions were passed, all textile shops reopened today. However, Dingxin is unwilling to accept these terms and has filed a lawsuit with the court this morning. After Inspector Chen visited the Dingxin shop for inspection, it is heard that a summons will be issued on the 9th. Therefore, this unrest is difficult to fully resolve.

Hangzhou

Victorious News from the Fourth Division in Zhejiang Suppressing Bandits

The Tenth Brigade of the Fourth Division of the National Army stationed in Zhejiang, after being ordered to be transferred to the border areas of Zhejiang and Jiangxi, Raozhou and Yushan, under the leadership of Brigade Commander Tang Enbo, has been working hard to suppress bandits, allowing the local area to be stabilized. Recently, the provincial government received a telegram from the brigade, stating that the main force of the Jiangxi Eastern Puppet Tenth Army's bandit Zhou Jianping, consisting of approximately four infantry regiments with 2,300 guns, had been harassing Ganlinjiangchao. The brigade dispatched the Twentieth Regiment, led by Regiment Commander Hu, with three battalions of soldiers to conduct a surprise attack overnight. At 7:00 a.m. the next morning, they engaged the bandits, defeating them after eight hours of intense fighting. Over 100 rifles were captured, 150-160 bandits were taken prisoner, and 700-800 bandits were killed. On our side, five officers and 50-60 soldiers were injured. The remaining bandits fled towards Mingyangguan. In addition to Regiment Commander Hu leading his troops in relentless pursuit, we hereby report this victory.

Ningbo

Strictly Prohibit Worker Riots

Yesterday morning, workers at the Hefeng Yarn Factory in Jiangdong, Ningbo, gathered and protested, demanding resumption of work. Upon receiving the news, the county government, fearing a major incident, immediately issued a notice prohibiting it. Furthermore, given the impact of this matter on industry and public order, a discussion was deemed necessary. Therefore, it was decided that a meeting would be held at the county government this morning, with representatives from the Party, police, and legal departments to discuss solutions. The transfer of cotton stored in the warehouse by the Hefeng Yarn Factory to a certain flower merchant is also being closely monitored.

Dayan Ao, Fenghua is Burned and Looted by Bandits

Dayan Ao, located in the Lilianshan area of Fenghua, about three miles below the Arrow Ridge, was suddenly attacked by approximately 60-70 bandits at around 8:00 a.m. on the 3rd of this month. They burned down over ten houses belonging to five families, including Liu Zhongyou's, and looted countless grains, livestock, and utensils. The total loss is estimated to be nearly ten thousand dollars.

Education News

Important News

Jiangsu Province's 20th Year Education Budget (5) Shi Zhang

(5) The End and the Beginning of Two Years

Outside the Jiangsu Province Education Expenditure Budget for the 19th year, there is a total of 348,890 yuan designated for "separate allocation." These funds were intended for the temporary expenses of various educational institutions, to be allocated by the Education Department as needed. As previously mentioned (see this newspaper on July 7th), after the 19th-year budget was finalized, the income could not cover the expenses, resulting in a significant shortfall. Consequently, these "separate allocation" temporary expenses had to be put on hold. However, due to the urgent and practical needs of various schools for construction, repairs, purchases, and equipment, they continued to plead their case despite the strained educational funding. The Education Funding Committee also expressed considerable sympathy. It was not until the 23rd meeting held on February 27th of this year that it was resolved that "the total amount of provincial education temporary expenses is 180,000 yuan, to be allocated by the Education Department," finally bringing the matter to a conclusion. Unexpectedly, after this decision was made, the Education Funding Management Office faced increasing financial difficulties in practice, and its ability to cope was exhausted. The repeated serious expressions of concern from the faculty and staff were all due to this. Naturally, at this time, the existing payable expenses could not be disbursed, let alone additional temporary expenses. Now that the 19th year has essentially passed, the schools are in the process of closing, and many have already advanced funds for construction and other expenses, which they urgently need to be reimbursed. Recognizing this, the Education Department, at the third meeting of the 20th year (July 3rd), based on the determined total amount, carefully examined the urgent needs of various institutions and made a comprehensive allocation, approving the amount and purpose of the temporary expenses for various educational institutions for the 19th year, and immediately issued orders to comply. This marks the end of the 19th-year budget and also serves as a precursor to the implementation of the 20th-year budget. The allocation of funds is listed below.

The Ministry of Education's Middle and Elementary School Curriculum Standards Editing and Equipment Committee originally scheduled its second meeting for the 13th, 14th, and 15th of this month at the Ministry of Education. Fujian Education Department Pays Attention to Vocational Guidance

The Fujian Education Department has recently been paying close attention to vocational guidance and is actively promoting cooperation with the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center. They intend to promote it using administrative power, starting with student guidance. They have specifically organized a Student Guidance Committee, chaired by Chief Zhong of the Education Department (Daozan). The following is an excerpt from its regulations: (1) The department has established the Fujian Education Department Student Guidance Committee to promote student guidance in schools throughout the province. (2) The members of the committee shall be appointed by the Director of the Education Department and shall consist of officials from the department and principals of secondary schools and above. (3) The committee shall have three to five executive committee members, who shall be elected by the members. (4) The committee shall have a chairman and a secretary, who shall be elected by the executive committee members. (5) The duties of the committee are divided into the following categories: (1) matters related to student guidance lectures; (2) matters related to the preparation of student intention surveys for higher education and employment guidance; (3) matters related to the editing of student guidance publications; (4) matters related to the collection of school regulations, admission prospectuses, and information on the content and organization of vocational institutions; (5) matters related to the liaison with higher education and vocational guidance institutions inside and outside the province; (6) matters related to the liaison and guidance of student guidance committee branches in schools throughout the province; (7) matters related to the investigation and adjustment of the actual content and personnel needs of schools and vocational institutions; (8) matters related to the establishment of a vocational placement office. (6) The committee may divide the work into several groups as needed and appoint responsible personnel to handle them. (7) The committee shall meet once a month. In case of necessity, the chairman may convene ad hoc meetings. (8) These regulations may be amended by the committee as necessary.

Important Remarks from Shen Siliang: Chinese Football Team to Organize Next Spring

| Decision to Participate in World Games in the US |

Opposes Philippine New Scoring Method

National Tennis Tournament This Autumn

During this spring's National Regional Football Tournament, representatives from various regions passed an important resolution: to send a Chinese football team to participate in the World Games held in the United States next August, and to select team members and organize the team between June and July this summer, before heading to Southeast Asia for matches and practice. However, this important resolution has remained silent. We, therefore, visited Shen Siliang, honorary director of the National Progressive Association, and recorded his remarks as follows:

Postponement to Next Spring for Team Organization

The Chinese football team will definitely cross the ocean to participate in the World Games in the US next fall. The original plan was to select players this summer. However, the Hong Kong side has already decided to send the Chung Hwa and Nanyang teams to Southeast Asia in advance. Therefore, the organization of the Chung Hwa team

Has to Be Temporarily Postponed

Southeast Asia, Java, and other places do not welcome too many teams to compete. However, the decision to go to the US remains unchanged. When the weather warms up slightly next spring, around March or April,

A Decision Will Be Made to Organize the Chinese Team

They will first go to Southeast Asia for matches and then return to the US, using this as practice and also raising funds for the trip, as the amount is considerable. If each team member requires US$1,000, it will cost over US$15,000 or US$16,000. Therefore, it is greatly hoped that

The Government Can Provide Relief

This matter will be seriously considered again at the National Games, and a complete resolution must be reached then.

Opposition to the Philippine New Scoring Method

Regarding the Far Eastern Games, the Philippines has proposed a change in the scoring method.

Contents of the New Scoring Method

In the future, all competitions will be scored, and the country with the most points, not the country with the most first-place finishes, will win the overall championship. The distribution of points will be based on the number of participants in each event. For example, track and field events, with many participants, will award 15 points to the track champion and the same for all-around. Basketball and tennis teams, with fewer players, will receive fewer points, with only 5 points awarded for first place. The total score of first, second, and third places in all competitions will determine the overall champion (detailed scoring and allocation methods are available).

The Philippine Reason for the Proposal

Is entirely for fairness. This way, the country with the most first-place finishes will not necessarily win the championship, giving countries with more second and third-place finishes a chance to win the overall championship. This proposal seems fair on the surface, but there are many practical drawbacks. Therefore, a letter expressing opposition has been sent, and Japan has also been informed of our stance.

The Chinese Reason for Opposition

If this method is adopted, the attitude of the Chinese towards various sports will greatly change. For example, tennis and basketball, with fewer points awarded, will have less impact on the overall championship and will be neglected. People might even think that volleyball is more important than tennis. If this misconception takes hold, the consequences will be disastrous, so we will further amend it.

A More Complete Proposal Is Made

Still adopting the scoring method, but awarding points of 5, 3, and 1 for first, second, and third place respectively. The champion team gets 5 points, the runner-up 3 points, and the third-place team 1 point. The calculation method is convenient, and various competitions will not be valued unequally. However, it is unknown whether it will be adopted.

National Tennis Tournament This Autumn

When asked about the ranking of national tennis players, the answer was that they were unaware of this matter. It would be difficult to determine the ranking during the National Games.

A Separate National Tennis Tournament Is Necessary

However, there are no preparations for the Chinese National Tennis Tournament, but

There Is a Planned National and Foreign Tennis Tournament

Inviting famous national and foreign tennis players to Shanghai for a large-scale competition, modeled after the example of the Invitation Tennis League in various countries, and also inviting famous players from Japan and other countries to Shanghai for exhibition matches, in order to benefit from observation.

The Time Is Late August or Early September

Around the time of the Rotary Cup International Tennis Tournament, or slightly later until September. Before the National Games, athletes from various regions will finish their competitions and can then go to Beijing to participate in the National Games.
