Free Talk

World Snippets

— Hai Ke

Plan to Advertise on Bald Heads

Europeans and Americans pay great attention to product advertising, often sparing no expense in pursuing it. Their advertising methods are also imaginative and innovative. Not long ago, a British advertising expert came up with a method of contacting telephone users one by one by telephone, reporting on various products, which soap is the most economical, which perfume is the most beautiful. However, this method is too troublesome, unnecessarily disturbing telephone users and easily causing annoyance. But recently, someone placed an advertisement in the newspaper, inviting twelve bald-headed gentlemen of high society for advertising purposes. That is truly wonderful. Their plan is to write product advertisements on those smooth bald heads, adding exquisite pictures. The ink used must be completely non-toxic and harmless to the scalp. After the advertisement is placed, they will be asked to go to theaters, concerts, dances, and churches. Just take off their hats, and the advertisement will be revealed. The power to attract attention is, of course, stronger than anything else. But whether anyone will respond is still uncertain.

Dark Skin May Be Able to Turn White

Japanese botanist Dr. Y. Noguchi recently returned from Brazil. He used electrical nourishment and glandular control methods on the natives in the forest, and there are already signs of success. According to him, when fully completed in the future, it can change races. Maybe it can turn the black skin of Negroes into white. The growth of a baby can also be controlled by human power. The length of the body and the width of the shoulders can be as desired. Whether these words can be done, let us wait and see.

Anecdotes of the Electric Capital

— Shi Yan Ye

Hollywood in the United States is known as the Electric Film Capital. A friend who traveled there shared his observations with me. I will describe one or two items for this publication.

The beauty of a woman, in addition to the beauty of the face, especially values the slenderness of the body. Only then can it be called beautiful in posture. To have a slender body, it is necessary to prevent the swelling of muscles. The invention of the fat regulation method is to seek to reduce the weight of the body for modern women. The beauty of the posture of movie stars is a necessary cultivation for their profession. Therefore, Hollywood actresses pay more attention to the method of removing swelling than ordinary people. Recently, it was learned that seaweed can reduce fat when eaten. Therefore, this vegetable has become an indispensable item for meals for general actresses. When they meet, they ask each other whether they have eaten seaweed today and use it as a gift. With the promotion of the electric stars, other women also eat it. Therefore, the sales of seaweed have greatly increased, and the price has also increased. It is said that most of this item is transported from Japan.

Hollywood has many companies that specialize in collecting strange people and things from around the world for use by various film companies and earn rent. Among them, strangely fat women, bearded women, and various freaks are completely collected. There is nothing strange that they do not have. All the rare birds and animals in the world are also available. In addition, there are other mythical things that are enough to make people see and be surprised. These strange things are the needs of the film from time to time. If the film company collects them one by one, it is really difficult to get what it wants. Speculators then started to store them to wait for them. Rent it to the application, demand supply, each get what they want, and also the way of both benefits.

A year ago, there were fewer than ten natural color cameras in the world. Today, Hollywood has thirty or forty. The development and progress of Electric Capital Films can be seen. As for the color films that use this machine to shoot, the output in the past two years is no less than hundreds.

There are no fewer than two thousand children among the actors in Hollywood. The age of these children ranges from just a few months to eighteen years. As the age is uneven, the physical strength is naturally strong and weak. The working hours must also be different. Generally, babies only work one hour a day and must be separated several times. Can not be continuous for it. Children of several ages work for four hours. There are four hours of rest and game offerings. Over fifteen or sixteen years old, the work is named eight hours. However, the rest and games in the middle also account for several hours.

Young Girl Who Recovered All Looted Goods

— Xiao

In recent years, Jiangbei counties have been plagued by bandits, and suppression has not been successful. Although the central government has specially set up appeasement officials, it is still unknown when the whole work can be completed. Wangjia Village near a town in Yancheng has a farmer named Wang, who is diligent and frugal throughout his life and has little savings. He has only one daughter under his knees, who is nine years old and is exceptionally smart. In addition, his wife's younger brother, Jia, is homeless due to the loss of both parents and lives in Wang's house all year round. There is also a farmhand, for a total of five people. The population is very simple. One night, someone in the same village married a wife. Wang and his wife went to the banquet together. At first, they planned to take their daughter with them, but the daughter suddenly said that she had a headache and had gone to bed early, so they left her at home. Unexpectedly, that night, six bandits suddenly came with open flames and sticks, destroying the door and entering. The wife's younger brother and the farmhand were all pale with fear and dared not speak. The bandits tied their hands and feet, and went straight into the girl's bedroom. They looked around and saw no one. There was only a young girl lying on the bed, so they called her up. The girl saw the situation and knew that they were bandits. Knowing that fear was useless, she calmly got out of bed. The bandit said, "Hey. Where are your parents?" The girl replied, "They went to a wedding feast." What do you want to do?" The bandit said, "We are here to collect debts. Where is the money hidden? You should know. Tell me the truth." The girl said, "All the money is hidden in this box. You can take it yourself." As she spoke, she pointed to a box and gave the key to the bandit. She lit a candle. The bandit got the key. He quickly moved the box pointed to the ground. He leaned over and opened it. The bandits leaned over to watch in turn. Sure enough, there were many oceans. Overjoyed. The girl held the candle and stood behind the bandits to illuminate them. The bandits still thought the girl was cute, but they didn't know that the girl had secretly dripped candle oil on the backs of the bandits, making secret marks. The bandit got the ocean and left. The girl secretly followed behind, observing the direction of their departure. Knowing that they were going to the town. She waited for her parents to return. When Wang and his wife returned home after hearing the news, the bandits had already gone far. The girl told them everything. Wang rushed to report to the police in the town, saying that the person with candle oil on his back was the bandit. He requested arrest. At that time, the sky was already bright. The bandits were hungry after not being comforted all night and went to a teahouse to wash and eat. Before long, a inspector came. He glanced at six people sitting together in the teahouse. Seeing their faces, they were not good people. He had suspicions, so he went inside to look at their backs. Sure enough, they all had candle oil on them. So he arrested them all. No one escaped. Searching their sides, the stolen money was all there, not a penny less.

Pillow

— Jian Fu

Explanation of the name The pillow is used to support the head when lying down. Because we always put our heads on the pillow when we sleep. Therefore, the pillow is closely related to our health. As the saying goes, "High pillow without worry." In fact, people who like high pillows mostly have curved waists and backs. Without heavy high pillows, their breathing is not smooth. Try to watch Westerners use low pillows or no pillows. Westerners value health, so their trunks are mostly straight. If you use a high pillow, it will hinder their breathing. It is also the effect of habit. As for our ordinary use of pillows, gas pillows are more suitable. Because the gas pillow can be transferred according to the amount of human head deviation. It can avoid the suffering of stiff neck. (When we go to bed at night, we feel pain in our necks during the day.) Farmers' pillows are mostly filled with grain husks or straw. Because farmers work hard all year round, and they rarely use their brains, there is no big problem. In fact, the attributes of grain husks and straw often produce mold in the heat of summer. Almost every summer, we sweat like Shen. The raw materials filled in the pillow absorb sweat. If you don't wash it frequently, the toxins of mold must be infected in the brain. It is most likely to cause brain disease. In addition, the floc pillow, which is most popular in the market recently, mostly uses the catkins of reeds. In fact, reeds and reed flowers are very warm. It is suitable for winter. Not applicable to summer. In addition to gas pillows, cool pillows are the most suitable for summer. In recent years, some people have invented water pillows. The method is to store ice juice or cold water in a ball bladder and put it inside the cool pillow. The next morning. Often feel that the brain is clear and easy to change. It is also a method of summer health. There is also an alarm pillow. It started with King Wusu Qian Yu. Yu was in the army. He never slept peacefully. Use a small round wooden pillow. When you fall asleep, you will stumble. Therefore, I got awakened. So named. Later, Zhuge Wuhou invented the cock-crowing pillow. Made of wood. Although the method of its construction has not been detailed. However, it does not show the intention of alerting and waking up. There is also a so-called fairy pillow. Kaiyuan Legacy. Guizi country entered a pillow. Warm and moist like jade. pillow it. Then, the ten continents, three islands, four seas and five lakes are all in dreams. Ming Emperor named it Youxian Pillow. Biography of the Immortals. Taishan elders. Shi Han Wudi toured east. Seeing his father plowing in the road. The white light on the head. Several feet high. Call and ask him. It is said that there are Taoists who teach ministers to make god pillows. The pillow has thirty-two holes. Corresponding to twenty-four gas. Eight holes should be eight winds. The minister is turning less and his teeth are more alive. The matter is not true. Gu Zhizhi. To be a help in talking.

Recently, the Wanbaoshan incident has turned into a bloody tragedy in which all Koreans are moved to kill our overseas Chinese. Obviously, it is a very serious issue in Sino-Japanese diplomacy. Other small capital trades. Very bland too. The power of the commercial field. Completely taken away by the Japanese. Do tenant farmers. Laborers. Suffering from the bullying of the Japanese. The jealousy and exclusion of the Korean people. Homeless overseas. Difficult to advance or retreat. Not only because of the weak national strength and the government's loss of protection. And the Japanese conspiracy. I wanted to expel the overseas Chinese early. Move the Korean people to Manchuria and Mongolia. Give the Korean peninsula in a clean color to his Japanese to operate. Rotary Club of Storytelling

??? (17)

— Xu Zhuodai

Ziliang thought about this, and he had no intention of working, so he hurried downstairs to take a look. Sure enough, the nanny had also followed this main mother. The door was open. Should I call them in? At this moment, there is no burnt rice, so of course they will not be willing to come in; should I let them go to see? I can only keep the door for them here; I want to go upstairs to work, I can only close the door. Ziliang thought for a while, and felt that it was safer to close the door, so he closed the door, put a bolt on it, and went back to the pavilion room himself.

He felt a little more settled in his heart, and then he started to work again. Suddenly someone knocked on the door. Have they come back? The sound of knocking on the door was very urgent, so Ziliang had to go downstairs and open the door. It turned out to be a postman.

"Express letter! Stamp it!"

Ziliang took the letter and looked at it. It was addressed to Ms. Pan Taoyue, and it was sent from Nanjing. He went back upstairs to get the stamp, stamped it, and when the postman left, he bolted the door again. He left the letter on the temple table in the living room and went upstairs himself.

He had only written two or three words, when someone knocked on the door again. Ziliang went downstairs listlessly and opened the door. It really was the two of them who had come back. Ziliang turned around and ran upstairs, but the wife followed behind:

"In broad daylight, why are you closing the door? Are you doing secret things inside?"

Ziliang didn't say a word, and when he reached the pavilion room, he sat down.

"What a grand funeral, it was beautiful! There were nine military bands; sixty-five cars: eighty-one wreaths: I don't know how many people sent it, men and women? The person who died was a woman, I heard she was the sister-in-law of a playboy."

As she said this, an envious look appeared on her face, and she stared at her husband:

"The sister-in-law of a playboy, how dignified? If the sister-in-law of a school teacher died, I'm afraid there would only be a few elegiac couplets!"

She said with emotion, seeing that her husband did not speak, she seemed very bored:

"I'm talking to you, why don't you make a sound?"

"If you open the door wide, people will run away, what if a thief breaks in and steals things, what can we do?"

"Does our family still have things for people to steal?"

US Government Report Was Beneficial to Short Positions

US cotton fell another 40 pounds yesterday. US cotton was weak due to the field report being beneficial to sellers, Wall Street being weak, and the harvest being smooth. The futures fell 37 to 44 pounds, and the spot fell 40 pounds. British cotton futures fell 20 to 21 points, and the spot fell 22 points. Egyptian cotton spot fell 25 points. Indian cotton was soft due to the weak market price at the opening in Liverpool. Pingguoer and Bailuoxi fell four rupees, and Aomula fell two rupees. The original telegram record is on the left (8th telegram)

US Cotton's First Government Report

Washington telegram on the 8th: The US cotton's first government report was released today by the Department of Agriculture's Estimation Bureau. The planted cotton area is 41,491,000 acres, a decrease of 4,324,000 acres compared to last year. The first eight years of cotton field area are also recorded on the left (unit: thousand acres)

Grain and Rice Market Increased Again

Not much new rice arrived at the New Gate yesterday. The total inventory of ship cargo was about 24,000 dan. Transactions between urban and rural areas were not very active. Su Chang thick japonica rice increased by one inch. At the moment, ordinary medium-grade goods are consistently tight. The source of thin rice has become increasingly scarce. Although the purchase appetite in this street is stable, the price has risen again by half an inch. Indica rice has excellent retail sales, and the price has not increased or decreased. Most of the foreign long-grain rice is used as a substitute for Saigon rice, so the local indica rice is scarce and stable. Glutinous rice rose slightly by a few cents, but buying interest was not strong. Each river factory's goods opened at more than 4,000 shi.

Yesterday, few boats came to the South Shanghai district, and the market was not smooth. The arrival of top-quality thin rice was lacking, and the bulk price immediately increased by two or three jiao. Ordinary goods also increased by a jiao or so. News from Qingpu said that the price of brown rice was becoming tighter, but people's hearts were looking up. Changxi's northern japonica rice and Su Tong's white japonica rice each increased by one inch. Ningbang purchased Nangang early rice, so the small amount of inventory was swept away, and the price was also looking up by nearly one inch. The future situation must be determined by the amount of arrivals. Lu Yang long-grain rice had light arrivals and sales, and the price did not increase or decrease. There were very few metamict colors, and there was no formal market to report.

Flour and Wheat Market Benefit from Torrential Rain

Yesterday, in the flour market, the opening of the market in the morning saw a generally calm situation across all months. With the price of foreign wheat continuing to fluctuate slightly, both insiders and outsiders were taking a wait-and-see approach, and trading was not very active. However, when the market opened in the afternoon, sentiment suddenly became agitated due to the hot and stuffy weather and unusual darkness, with predictions of more heavy rain. At this point, sentiment had already been shaken. After the market opened, the rain gradually intensified, no less than the heavy rain of a few days ago. The mainland traders believed that various places had already been flooded, and with this heavy rain, the situation would inevitably be more difficult to manage. Therefore, buying interest was unusually strong, gradually increasing and showing a strong momentum. Observing the subsequent steps, due to the excessive rain, it is feared that it will still agitate sentiment. Currently, Flour "Soldier Ship" is increased by 3 cents according to the standard, and Fufeng "Red and Blue Car" is increased by 1 cent. As a result, the current month rose by half a cent compared to the previous day, August rose by 2 cents, September rose by 1.75 cents, and October to December each rose by 2 cents, it is said.

Yesterday, in the wheat market, after the opening of the market in the morning, the situation across all months generally tended to be stable. Because the price of foreign wheat was fluctuating slightly, and the weather was still good, the opening prices of each session were not much different from the previous day. However, when the market opened in the afternoon, the sky was dark, indicating impending rain, so sentiment rebounded again, with speculators trying their best to cover their positions, and bulls aggressively buying non-stop, leading to simultaneous gains in both near and distant terms. Later, as the rain became heavier, sentiment improved even more, especially for distant terms. Observing this kind of rising trend, it is entirely driven by the rain. Because foreign wheat has been falling for several days, the overseas wheat market is ultimately tending towards surplus. If the environment is ignored and prices are still aggressively raised, there will eventually be setbacks. As a result, the current month rose by 2 cents compared to the previous day, August rose by 3 cents, September rose by 4 cents, October rose by 5 cents, November rose by 6 cents, and December rose by 4 cents. The current wheat market has become stable, as factories have chosen to purchase at higher prices, no longer as silent as before. More than 4,000 packages of wheat from Danyang, Benniu, Zhenjiang, Penglai, Shuangfeng, Kunshan, Jiaxing, Liuhe, Nanjing, Hezhou, Taizhou, Anting, Gaoyou, etc., were purchased by Fuxin, Shenda, Huafeng, etc., it is said.

Silk and Tea Japanese Firms Actively Purchase New Silk

Strong Interest in Double Cocoon Silk

Boiled Cocoons Also See Demand

The spring cocoon market in various provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang has long ended, and summer cocoons have already entered the market. New silk from silkworms is now being shipped to Shanghai one after another. Silk merchants are submitting samples to various foreign firms for testing to negotiate new transactions. Recently, Japanese firms such as Mitsui, Harada, and Eika have shown considerable interest in new silk. There is strong interest in double cocoon silk, and boiled cocoons also have demand. It is heard that there are already five to six hundred dan of double cocoon silk, and the transaction price is higher than old cocoons. Superior quality goods require 58-59 taels, it is said.

European and American Silk Sales Become Increasingly Stagnant

Yesterday, the Shanghai foreign firms' silk market was stagnant, as overseas markets showed no sign of recovery in silk sales, and silk prices continued to be weak. Telegrams from Shanghai were still rarely forwarded to Shanghai. Yesterday, only Lianna imported ten packages of white filature silk into Shanghai, and Taihe and others imported thirty-five packages of new dried silk, with prices remaining stable, it is said.

Tunxi Green Tea Harvest Reduced

Tunxi is an important town in southern Anhui and also a tea market center. There are more than forty tea processing firms. Recently, due to weak tea shipments from various routes, supply cannot meet demand, leading to a gradual and firm rise in tea prices, from 60 yuan per dan to over 90 yuan. Currently, tea merchants and vendors have no tea leaves left in hand, and most firms have already closed down due to lack of tea to buy. According to current reliable surveys and estimates, the total amount of Tunxi green tea this year is only slightly over 30,050 dan, a decrease of 50% compared to last year. The scarcity of tea is unprecedented in more than ten years, it is said.

New Arrival of American Standard Square Nails

According to news from foreign firms yesterday, the American standard square nails, which have been in short supply for many days, will have over 4,000 barrels imported next Wednesday or Thursday. The purchasers are said to be Shenchang, Anli, Meikang and other foreign firms, while domestic purchasers are lead firms and construction teams in the North Suzhou Road area, it is said.

White Lead Sheet No. 6 Sales Active

The sales of white lead sheets fluctuate between brisk and sluggish, so the decoration of various colors in the market is also sometimes good and sometimes bad. In recent days, No. 5 and No. 6 have seen many transactions due to purchases by battery factories, with the market price estimated at 25.5 taels per dan. It is heard that factories and merchants have been making batch purchases for days, and although it rained lightly yesterday, the transactions still reached more than 180 barrels, it is said.

Black Iron Sheet No Stock in Near Term

Regarding the 18-gauge black iron sheet futures purchased by domestic firms in the previous month, according to news from foreign firms, the factory has telegraphed that there is no stock in the near term and it will be delayed for four weeks before there is stock available for shipment to Shanghai. Therefore, local firms, hearing this news, are in good spirits, and the market price has increased by several cents, estimated at 11.5 taels per dan, it is said.

Piece Goods Show Slight Increase

Yesterday, the piece goods market rebounded due to the rise in the gold market. Osaka's fixed prices all rose by 2.5 to 5 cents, so the spot market showed a slightly firming trend. "Four Gentlemen" straight tribute woolen cloth was 3 qian, 1 fen, 7.5 li, Moganshan was 3 qian, 6.5 fen, and Lieyan Muqiu was 3 qian, 6 fen, 7.5 li. Spot goods of plain foreign yarn are increasingly scarce, and Dianqiu Han has reached 10 taels and 1.5 qian yesterday. Brands such as Huameiren, Xiaomeiren, and Shuangtonglu seem to be impossible to find. White crepe remains stable, and Guanghua Se Ting has been arriving in Shanghai successively, with prices opening at 2 qian, 6.5 to 7 fen. Yuehua Velvet is slightly firmer, with large patterns at 2 qian, 5 fen, and medium patterns at 2 qian, 4 fen. Sesame Velvet from Sichuan, Xuzhou, and other regions has strong demand. Niao Meiren is 2 qian, 5 fen, 7.5 li, and Heping is 3 qian, 2 fen. Striped Fuchou and blue striped Se Ting are being cleared out daily due to the approaching off-season. Printed linen and printed Se Ting are being sought after by large buyers, with prices around 2 qian. Fine twill is difficult to rally due to the abundance of supply. The ordering of Western striped Fuchou has been unusually active recently, with all-yarn around 4 qian and single-yarn, single-thread around 5 qian, it is said.

Sugar Market Raw Sugar and White Sugar Open at Over 3,000 Bags

Marked Prices Show Slight Increase

Yesterday's sugar market telex from the production area reported that the spot price of Cuban sugar remained unchanged. New York sugar futures for all months fell back by 1 cent. The spot price of Javanese sugar also lacked fluctuations. In the marked price session of the association market, due to the rising exchange rate, sentiment improved, and buying interest increased slightly. The transaction price for Dutch No. 24 raw sugar was 10 taels and 7 qian, with extremely short supply for delivery. No. 20 medium white sugar was 10 taels and 3 qian, with the highest quality at 10 taels and 4 qian. The market shape was extremely beautiful. The Japanese sugar market also rose slightly, with N mark at 10 taels and 7.5 qian, SH mark at 10 taels and 6 qian to 2.5 fen, J mark at 11 taels and 1 qian, YT mark at 10 taels and 7 qian, YP mark at 11 taels and 5 qian, YRO mark at 10 taels and 5.5 qian, TK mark at 10 taels and 7.5 qian, TM mark at 10 taels and 6 qian 2.5 fen, AE mark at 11 taels and 1 qian, and Taikoo B mark at 11 taels and 1 qian. There were few deliveries, and the asking price for the next session was 11 taels and 1.5 qian. Trading was still active, and the market shape was quite brisk. Jianji Hao opened with 2,500 bags of raw sugar, and Deda Hao sold 900 bags, with prices all at 10 taels and 7 qian. The market was selling firmly, and Zhenxiang, Huaxin and other firms were holding back and not selling, it is said.

Northern and Southern Goods Longkou Vermicelli Market Price Inverted

The transport of Longkou vermicelli has led to low inventory in the area, and purchase prices are rising. According to recent correspondence, each package has reached 32 taels, and the cost to Shanghai is over 24 taels per dan. Therefore, local goods are also holding tight. Yesterday, a few opened at 23 taels and 2 qian, and the market generally requires 24 taels before being willing to open again. However, local sales have not been brisk, with trading at 23.5 taels being rare, so the market price has become inverted. However, judging from the situation, future sales will eventually turn around. The cost of purchases has increased, and inventory is low, so the market will undoubtedly rise in the future.

National Army Swearing-in Ceremony for the Northern Expedition Anniversary Assembly

Various Circles Held a Meeting Yesterday

Yesterday was the 5th anniversary of the National Revolutionary Army's Swearing-in Ceremony for the Northern Expedition. The Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters specifically convened people from all walks of life in the city to hold a commemorative meeting. Over 800 representatives attended. The details are recorded below:

Attending Representatives

Chen Kecheng, Zhang Yinhuai, Chen Xunyu, Wang Da from the Municipal Government, Jin Yu, Zhou Baoli from the Garrison Command, Yang Peiwen from the Municipal Education Bureau, Xiang Junxian, Miao Wenyi from the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Yao Yuanding from the Shanghai Local Court, Ding Shuhua from the Shanghai Customs Supervisory Office, Tian Heqing, Xue Wenyuan from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, Wu Puquan from the Municipal Finance Bureau, Zhang Junpu from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Xun Fei from the Shanghai Postal Administration, Li Junfeng from the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau, Yang Yuanchang, Chen Xiji, Chen Hao, Wang Jiqing from the Municipal Land Bureau, Zhang Yunge from the Municipal Public Works Bureau, Zhong Zhiqi from the Municipal Health Bureau, and over 800 representatives from various labor unions, organizations, and levels of the Party Headquarters.

Chairman's Report

Fellow Representatives, Fellow Comrades, today is the fifth anniversary of the National Revolutionary Army's oath to launch the Northern Expedition. In the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, our Party swore to launch the Northern Expedition, which was of great significance in the revolutionary process. Because of the Northern Expedition sworn five years ago, we have today's situation. Although today's situation is still far from our ideal state, if we are united from top to bottom, work together, and continue the spirit of the Northern Expedition, the National Revolution will not be difficult to succeed, and the Three People's Principles will eventually be realized. Since the Opium War, our country has suffered from the heavy oppression of international imperialism externally, and the ravages and destruction of feudal forces internally. The national economy and people's livelihood have become increasingly precarious. Before the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, our Party had worked hard to fight against imperialism and feudal forces, but it ultimately failed. There are three reasons for this. Before the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, the Party's organization was particularly loose. There was no close connection between the Party and its members, between Party members and the people, and between Party members. Once an incident occurred, it relied on personal enthusiasm or the righteous indignation of a few people. There was no strict organization, and even less planned action. It is no wonder that it failed. This is one reason. Before the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, the Party's military force had not been cultivated. It often used troops who expressed sympathy for the revolution to fight against counter-revolutionaries. Whether military training was mature or not was a secondary matter. Whether the construction of ideological beliefs and revolutionary confidence was deep or not had a great impact. It was easy to sympathize for a while, but it was not surprising that incidents of defection and betrayal occurred during a long struggle in hardship. Before the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, it was not that there was no Northern Expedition, but the reason for repeated failures was the lack of basic revolutionary military force. This is the second reason. The National Revolution is by no means the business of a few people, nor can it be successful with the struggle of a few people. Before the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, the Party's work focused on assassination, uprisings, and arousing the people to work together. No attention was paid. As a result, the people were mostly ignorant of the truth about our Party and mostly regarded it as a mob. The easy failure of the revolution was a major reason. This is the third reason. After the reorganization of our Party in the thirteenth year of the Republic of China, it swept away the accumulated malpractices of the past. In terms of military affairs, it specially established the Whampoa Military Academy to specialize in cultivating revolutionary military force. In less than two years, its strength was greatly prepared. Therefore, the Central Committee of our Party decided to swear to launch the Northern Expedition on July 9th of the fifteenth year of the Republic of China. At that time, the weather was extremely hot, and sweat poured down like rain, but the revolutionary soldiers' enthusiasm for killing the enemy and achieving results was also as exciting as the climate. Hundreds of thousands of brave soldiers, under the leadership of Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek, marched north in a mighty and grand manner. In a few months, they conquered the borders of Guangdong and Guangxi, secured the important towns of Hunan and Hubei, captured Jiangxi, and recovered Jiangsu and Zhejiang. The momentum was unprecedented. After recovering Shanghai, the Central Committee of our Party realized that the Red Bandits' conspiracy to usurp the Party and the country was fully exposed, so it resolutely and decisively carried out the purge. Many of the comrades present today were working in the secret era. Recalling the cruelty of the Communist bandits' oppression of the comrades of our Party in those years is heartbreaking. The arrogance of the Communist bandits in Shanghai was infuriating. Fortunately, Mr. Wu, Cai, Li, and Chiang Kai-shek recognized the Party's crisis, made a choice in an instant, and made a grand plan in an instant. They expelled the Communist Party and punished the fierce and stubborn according to the law, so that sovereignty would not fall into the hands of others, and the Party and the country would turn from danger to safety. Those who read the Party history of our Party and the national history of our country should applaud it. In the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, the Communist bandits were wiped out, and the rear was stabilized. The Central Committee resumed the second phase of the Northern Expedition. Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek again led a large army and marched north again. Unexpectedly, after recovering Jinan, the Japanese imperialists were mad and massacred our National Army. The May 3rd Jinan Massacre occurred. Diplomat Cai Gongshi was killed, Foreign Minister Huang Yingbai was insulted, and tens of thousands of soldiers and civilians were killed. The loss of property was no less than tens of millions. The situation was tragic, and the disaster was unprecedented in ancient and modern times, both at home and abroad. Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek endured the humiliation and pain at this critical moment and detoured the Northern Expedition, because he did not want to fall into the cunning scheme of the Chinese and Japanese. The people of the country were filled with righteous indignation and grief, but they remained calm and waited for the opportunity, because they did not want to disrupt the overall situation. Relying on the bravery of the soldiers to kill the enemy, the Northern Warlords finally collapsed and fled east and west. The peaceful and unified situation that the Prime Minister had eagerly hoped for was finally achieved. The reason why the success of this Northern Expedition was so rapid, and the reason why its achievement was so great, was due to Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek's skillful command, the revolutionary soldiers' brave fight against the enemy, and the hard work of the Party's propaganda work, and the assistance of the revolutionary people. Therefore, in addition to warmly supporting Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek, who has worked hard, and commemorating the revolutionary martyrs who died for the country, it is even more necessary to strengthen the Party's work and awaken the revolutionary consciousness of the people. It has been two years since the success of the Northern Expedition. The suffering of the people should be alleviated, and the international status should be raised. However, to this day, the people's livelihood is still haggard, and the country is still in danger. The reason for this is the revival and rebellion of new and old warlords. In the recent two years, there was Tang Shengzhi and Zhang Fakui before, and Yan Xishan and Feng Yuxiang after. Now there is the Guangdong Incident. The misfortunes have come one after another, and the Red Bandits jumping around in the southeast are even more a cause for concern for us. Therefore, the awakened and revolutionary people should recognize the difficult situation since the establishment of the National Government, and should work hard on the following three points, grasp the working line of the revolution, so as to complete the great mission of the times. First, recognize the Party's program and platform, strive to support the Central Committee, and complete the great cause of the revolution. The Guangdong side and all reactionaries often slander the Central Committee and accuse Chiang Kai-shek of dictatorship. In fact, whether the Central Committee's recent measures are accurate, and whether Chairman Chiang Kai-shek is a dictator, are facts that are obvious to all. There is no need for partiality. Since Chairman Chiang Kai-shek devoted himself to the revolution, his contributions and progress to the revolutionary cause have been demonstrated to the world. There is no need for boasting. Seeking perfection and blaming is indeed the way of the virtuous. If there is another meaning, and a crime is added, then how should those of us who love the Party and the country recognize their cunning schemes, expose their conspiracies, and not be influenced by their instigation? To save China today, to relieve the people's suffering today, there is no other way but to support the Central Committee and ensure peaceful unification. Second, strive to eliminate the Red Bandits. The disasters caused by the Red Bandits in China, and the cruelty of killing the people, are unprecedented at home and abroad. The people of Jiangxi have been haggard and moaning under the ravages of the Red Bandits for more than a year. The people in the southeastern provinces who have been killed, looted, and plundered by the Red Bandits still remember it as if it were yesterday. If this is not extinguished, the troubles in Lu will not end. Now Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek is personally leading the troops to suppress the Red Bandits. The elimination of the Red Bandits will naturally not be a problem. However, the Red Bandits often use lower-level people as a vanguard. The people who are young and ignorant actually recognize the thief as their father and are willing to be driven. This is truly lamentable and heartbreaking. It is hoped that the revolutionary people will bear the greatest responsibility, do their best, save our country, save our nation, and even save our foolish people who have gone astray. Third, the Wanbaoshan Incident was instigated by the Japanese imperialists. The people of the country see it as clearly as fire. The Japanese imperialists are still pretending to be stupid and pretending not to know. It is truly not worth laughing at. From this, it can be seen that the only great enemy of our country's National Revolution, and the greatest obstacle to our country's freedom and equality, is the Japanese imperialists. To achieve peace in the East, it is necessary to overthrow Japanese imperialism. Without eradicating the Japanese imperialists, it is not enough to wash away the shame of the East. Economic non-cooperation has been repeatedly mentioned by my brothers at previous commemorative meetings. I hope that the people of this city will not forget it either. The Korean people willingly act as tools and provide weapons for riots. In addition to deeply sympathizing with them, we also hope that they will realize that they are always being pleased by the enemy and grieved by the onlookers. Today, in the midst of boundless excitement, I report the above points, and I hope that the representatives present will pay attention to them. Finished. Then Chen Kecheng and others successively gave speeches. The speeches were long and abbreviated.

Reactions to the Sino-Foreign Jointly Operated Sugar Factory

Representatives of the Sugar Industry Go to Beijing to Petition

The Shanghai Sugar Industry Association previously heard that the Ministry of Industry was borrowing money from foreign merchants to establish a sugar factory, but the draft agreement that was drawn up contained many provisions that would lose national sovereignty. It telegraphed the Ministry of Industry to inquire about it. The ministry then sent a vague reply, which aroused even more suspicion among the industry. Subsequently, the industry tried every means to investigate the contents of the draft agreement. It learned that the agreement did contain many points that would humiliate the country and harm the people. The members of the industry were extremely indignant and held a general meeting to discuss the matter. As a result, the various points in the draft agreement where the foreign merchants were deceiving, cunningly taking advantage, and rapaciously seizing were listed in detail and presented in a memorial. Zheng Zenan, Yang Wenshao, and Jiang Yachen were appointed to go to Beijing on the 7th to petition the Legislative Yuan, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Industry, urging them to correct the contract in order to maintain national sovereignty and save losses. The petition of the association is recorded below:

To the Legislative Yuan

Presented to Petition for the Correction of the Ministry of Industry's

Contract with Foreign Merchants to Borrow Money to Establish a Sugar Factory, and Suggestions to Completely Nationalize it in order to Save Losses and Maintain National Sovereignty. Your humble association previously heard that the Ministry of Industry was borrowing money from sugar merchants in Cuba to establish a sugar factory. Because the matter was of great importance to national sovereignty and the sugar industry, it telegraphed the Ministry of Industry to inquire about the truth of the matter. It then received a vague reply from the Ministry, and it was even more suspicious. Then, newspapers continued to report on the matter, detailing it in great detail. The Ministry of Industry has signed a draft contract with the Havana International Sugar Company of Cuba to borrow money to establish a sugar factory. It has been decided by the 222nd Central Political Conference and sent to your esteemed Yuan for review. Your humble association believes that the matter is of great importance to our country's industry and is closely related to the future of the sugar industry. It did not dare to remain indifferent and took action. According to rumors, the contents of the draft contract contain many points that would humiliate the country and harm the people. Upon hearing this, it was at a loss. It is respectfully submitted that the China National Sugar Manufacturing Company went bankrupt due to poor management. If the state-run sugar factory is again controlled and monopolized by foreign merchants, and repeats the mistakes of the National Sugar Manufacturing Company, then there is no hope for the revitalization of our country's sugar manufacturing industry, and the principle of promoting sugar cane planting as a basis for expanding sugar manufacturing is even more hopeless. The huge and alarming losses can also not be recovered. How can one fully express its impact on the rise and fall of national sovereignty, and the rise and fall of agriculture, industry, and commerce? The advantages and disadvantages of industry and commerce are numerous and cannot be fully understood except by those who have personally experienced them. Your humble association has been engaged in this industry for a long time and is very familiar with it. It is deeply concerned and cannot remain silent. Therefore, it is using its own insights to supplement the profound, and listing the harmful points of the contract, and respectfully presenting them to your esteemed Yuan one by one. (1) The sugar factory is nominally state-run, but the hiring and administration are completely subject to interference, and the finances are subject to control and supervision. (2) The interest on the loan is 8% per week. Compared with the ordinary interest rate of 2-3% in European and American countries, it is undoubtedly subject to harsh exploitation. (3) The purchase of raw materials and the export of products are handled by it alone, then the great power of buying and selling the sugar factory is abandoned without reservation. It is given the power to manipulate and monopolize, and to satisfy its endless desires. (4) Regarding the price of purchasing raw materials, it is recognized that the market price at that time is the standard. However, the market price is the surface of each country's market. Its actual price depends on the amount of purchasing power, and the special low-price black market. If the market price is used as the standard, then this raw material may not be able to obtain cheap goods, but instead secretly consume unknown amounts. (5) The purchase of raw materials and the sale of products are handled by it. According to the contract, the money used in and out is about 10 taels of silver per picul. If the sugar factory produces 1,000 tons per month, and the annual production is 330,000 tons except for one month for machine maintenance, then the money obtained will be more than 4 million yuan. Calculated over 20 years, it amounts to more than 80 million yuan, and the interest on this loss is not yet calculated. (6) The entire machine for building a sugar factory with a daily output of 1,000 tons is also purchased by its exclusive authority. The cost of this entire machine is about more than 10 million. According to the custom of the business community, the rebate is 10%, then it can also pocket more than 1 million in huge money, and the embezzlement of the machine price can be imagined. (7) The person who signed on behalf of the merchant, Mr. J.H. Laud, is now organizing the China International Sugar Company as the sole agency for selling the products of the factory. It is said that its sales method is mainly based on local distribution. However, this kind of distribution method has many drawbacks and is most unfavorable to the sugar factory. Before the factory's official announcement of price increases and decreases, distributors collude internally and externally, and can inquire and know the price increase first and sell later, and the price decrease first and sell later. Even if it is inspected, it will definitely be bribed and concealed. The complete failure of Jardine Matheson's sugar transportation and the gradual decline of Taikoo's sugar transportation are all due to this. Japanese sugar and Javanese sugar have abandoned this distribution method, so they can travel smoothly without hindrance. If it is allowed to sell it by distribution, then the losses suffered between price increases and decreases will be numerous. (8) The loan is US$5 million. The Ministry issues corresponding Class A bonds to repay the loan. In addition, it also requires the Ministry to issue another 15 million yuan of Class B bonds to guarantee the repayment of the sugar money. This kind of Class B bonds is guaranteed by all the property of the sugar species, that is, the land, machines, warehouses, and all other buildings, and all the refined and raw sugar stored inside and outside the factory are double-guaranteed. The right to sell products is also controlled by them, and its price is tantamount to its triple guarantee. Judging from its intentions, the contract has already been used to accumulate the capital for aggression, and the sugar factory must fail, fearing that the sugar money will not be secured, so it has this requirement. The intention in this is even more obvious. Therefore, it is like holding guns and wearing steel armor, defending against the Ministry of Industry again and again, and the national system and credit are almost lost. Looking at this contract as a whole, people are knives and boards, and we are fish and meat. There are a hundred harms and no benefits, and the most important right to buy and sell is handed over to others to control, which is a violation of the principle of state-owned enterprises. Moreover, on the surface, it is still using foreign capital to develop industries, but in fact, it is turning it into exploitation and giving it an opportunity for aggression. If the sugar factory fails in the future, it has already grabbed enough and left, and the losses will be borne by the people of our country. Humiliating the country and impoverishing the people is too much to say. Furthermore, the population of Cuba is only 3.5 million, which is only equal to the population of a corner of Shanghai, and it is also a poor country. How can it have the financial resources to lend to others? It is nothing more than using this to implement its aggressive economic ambitions. Our country is a vast country with a large population, and it is shameful to rely on it for the sugar industry and to be cunningly seized and exploited. This is something that our 500 million people cannot bear. It is earnestly requested that your esteemed association grant it a review, and strictly correct this contract. At the very least, the rights to equipment and sales should be completely under our country's autonomy, so as to strengthen national sovereignty and save losses, or fundamentally cancel the contract, and completely nationalize the establishment of sugar factories. All the capital of state-owned enterprises should be filled by the Ministry of Finance issuing corresponding public bonds. The principal repayment fund for these public bonds should be added to the national sugar import tax. Our people would rather bear the burden of increased tariffs than see the decline of national sovereignty and allow others to invade and endanger the foundation of the country. Your humble association is deeply concerned and eager to speak, and dares to express its feelings and petitions without considering being presumptuous. I earnestly hope that your esteemed Yuan will make a decisive decision and approve what is requested. The country will be fortunate, and the sugar industry will be fortunate. Respectfully presented.

To the Ministry of Industry

Presented to Petition for the Amendment of the Contract with Foreign Merchants to Borrow Money to Establish a Sugar Factory, and Suggestions to Completely Nationalize it in order to Save Losses and Maintain National Sovereignty. Your humble association previously heard that your esteemed ministry was borrowing money from sugar merchants in Cuba to establish a sugar factory. Because the matter was of great importance to national sovereignty and the sugar industry, it telegraphed your esteemed ministry to inquire about the truth of the matter. It then received a reply from the ministry, which was encouraging. I was pleased and celebrated the future of our country's sugar industry. Then, newspapers continued to report on the matter, detailing it in great detail... (omitted in the middle) I earnestly hope that your esteemed ministry will approve what is requested. The country will be fortunate, and the sugar industry will be fortunate. (omitted below) (The text presented to the Executive Yuan is the same as that of the Legislative Yuan, omitted).

Supervisory Yuan Commissioner Talks About the Recent Situation of Inner and Outer Mongolia

Our country's northwest frontier is vast and sparsely populated, with abundant resources. However, due to inconvenient transportation and years of domestic war, there is little close contact with each other. Since the end of the Qing Dynasty, the relationship between the country and the border has declined day by day, from close to distant, from distant to far, and to this day, it is almost completely isolated. Although the domestic intellectual classes have recently become aware of this, due to the inconvenience of transportation, they still cannot avoid the feeling of being at the ends of the earth. A member of the Central Supervisory Yuan, who recently came to Shanghai from Mongolia, met with a reporter from the New Voice Society at a hotel and talked about the recent situation of Inner and Outer Mongolia in great detail. The following is specially recorded for the reference of those who pay attention to the border areas.

Inner Mongolia

Political Overview

Inner Mongolia is divided into six leagues: Yikezhao, Ulanqab, Xilingol, Ju Ud, Josutu, and Jerim. Under the league, there are banners. The number of banners depends on the size of the league. In addition to the leagues, there are also independent banners and special banners, such as Alxa, Xishimete, Ejin, Torghut, Qiqihar, Yikemiankan, Hulunbuir, Solunbagu, etc., which are not under the jurisdiction of the leagues. The league is the highest organ. Each league has a league chief, and under him there is a jasagh, which is the official position of the banner, who governs the banners under his jurisdiction. Although the league chief is one level higher than the jasagh, he does not have political power. The judiciary also has certain legal provisions, which are not like the Dalai Lama of Tibet who exercises power at will. The current law is the Mongolian Law promulgated by the Qing Dynasty's Lifan Yuan, with slight improvements.

Military Organization

The military uses "zhangjing" as the military leader, whose authority is like that of the commander-in-chief in the interior. The army is entirely cavalry, without infantry or artillery. The number of troops is also uncertain, depending on the size of the banner. Large banners have two or three thousand troops, while small banners have only one or two hundred. Among them, there are also Han people serving as officers and soldiers. However, in Xilingol League, because the area belongs to nomadic areas and Han people are extremely rare, there are no Han people in the army.

Agriculture, Commerce, and Transportation

In terms of commerce, in addition to Han merchants dealing in tea, furs, etc., the Mongolians have no other commerce to speak of. Apart from nomadic life, in recent years, some people have gradually engaged in agriculture, but the number is very small and it is not developed. In terms of transportation, only Yikezhao League and Ulanqab League are more convenient, but compared to the interior, they are still far behind. In addition to horses, camels, ox carts, camel carts, and sedan cars from Zhangbei, there is no other way to travel. In terms of postal and telecommunications, only the postal service has some facilities, but they are mostly imperfect.

Religious Belief

According to rumors in the interior, the Mongolians completely believe in Buddhism. In fact, the Mongolians' belief is also quite free. For example, some Mongolians believe in Islam and Christianity. Currently, the influence of Islam is quite strong, especially in Alxa and Qilu banners. Christianity has very little influence. Although those who believe in Buddhism are quite devout to lamas, lamas in Mongolia still cannot control political power.

Situation of Han People

There are many Han people living in Inner Mongolia. Yikezhao and Ulanqab leagues have the most. The proportion of Mongolians and Han people in these two leagues is almost two to eight. They are mainly engaged in agriculture and commerce, with more farmers than merchants. The relationship between Mongolians and Han people is quite harmonious.

Outer Mongolia

Formation of the New Government

Outer Mongolia seceded from China and became independent in the ninth year of the Republic of China, and was incited by the Third International to establish the so-called Mongolian People's Republic. Its political organization is the People's Representative Assembly, which is held once a year, around August in the autumn, as the highest organ. The Assembly re-elects one standing committee member every year, with about 21 or more members (this is equivalent to an executive committee member, because the Mongolian translation means standing committee). From the 20-odd standing committee members, 5-7 members are re-elected to the standing office committee (this is the standing committee). From the standing office committee, one chairman is re-elected to manage all affairs of the Mongolian Republican government. Under him is a prime minister, who is the executive office committee chairman and issues all orders. Under him, there are nine ministries: interior affairs, foreign affairs, finance, transportation, military affairs, justice, agriculture and commerce, and education. Each ministry has one minister, who is appointed by the standing committee members elected by the People's Representative Assembly. Under the government, there are tribal governments (equivalent to provincial governments), and under the tribal governments, there are banner governments. Their organizations are similar to the government of the Mongolian Republic.

New Army Organization

Although the organization of the new army is not known in detail by outsiders, it is generally considered more advanced than before. Even in terms of weaponry, it should have everything it needs. Furthermore, the Outer Mongolian army has fully adopted conscription. All those reaching military age, except the disabled, have no way to avoid it. They stipulate that the period of military service for the people is two years. After the expiration of the term and discharge, they must still respond to the call of the Banner government in their area every year for half a month of training. Those who have held ministerial or other important positions, if they are not in office when conscripted, must also respond to the call, otherwise they will not be tolerated by the government. Therefore, since the implementation of conscription in Outer Mongolia, the entire territory is now militarized.

Compulsory Education

In addition to establishing schools in every tribe and Banner, Outer Mongolia is also implementing compulsory education. All boys and girls must attend school at the age of six, otherwise their parents will be fined. The government also has appropriate remedies for the poor and those without the means. As a result, the opening of the intelligence of the people of Outer Mongolia has been quite impressive over the past ten years. In the past, Inner Mongolians ("Oukuli," meaning stupid cows) ridiculed Outer Mongolia, but now they are ridiculed by Outer Mongolia.

Supervising Officials

In addition to the Mongolian Republican Government, there is also an Internal Security Bureau, which is like the Supervisory Yuan of our current government. The central agency has extremely broad powers. Its duty is specifically to accept people's impeachments against certain officials. After the Internal Security Bureau accepts a request to impeach an official, it does not notify the official, nor does it ask about the truth or falsehood of the matter. It first arrests the accused official and then determines whether a crime has been committed. If a crime has indeed been committed, then severe punishment will be imposed. Otherwise, they will be reinstated to their original position, and the government will publicly declare that they were falsely accused, so that their reputation will not be damaged.

Russian Influence

Soviet Russia does not have any significant influence in Outer Mongolia, contrary to what is reported in the newspapers. The Outer Mongolian authorities also do not allow them to have any influence. Apart from Russians who are automatically employed by the government, there are no Russians holding political power in Outer Mongolia. Furthermore, Russians who commit crimes in Mongolia are treated the same as other foreigners and punished accordingly. I (a certain supervisory committee member claiming) have seen the Mongolian judiciary execute one Japanese person and one Russian person on the day of execution for crimes committed, and the Japanese and Russian authorities did not dare to do anything.

Left and Right Factions

Within Outer Mongolia, since three years ago, there has been a division into left and right factions, but the struggle is not very fierce yet. Recently, the left faction has gained considerable power. It is not yet known what changes will occur in the future.

Expelling Han Chinese

The expulsion of Han Chinese from Outer Mongolia and the confiscation of their property did indeed happen, but not completely. Most of the Han Chinese who were expelled were idlers and vagrants. The confiscated property was also the property of these people. The remaining Han merchants, such as those dealing in fur and tea, remain in Mongolia and have not been expelled.

Foreigners Entering the Country

Currently, Han Chinese and other foreigners can still enter Outer Mongolia, but they must go through certain procedures, such as obtaining a passport, obtaining permission from the Mongolian government, and inspection of luggage. There are customs offices on the Russian-Mongolian border, and checkpoints on the borders of Inner Mongolia, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe. Goods brought into the country are subject to taxation. Inner Mongolians who wish to enter the country must also go through the above procedures.

Currency Situation

Recently, Outer Mongolia also has new currency in circulation. Internally, it is based on silver, and externally, such as for collecting tariffs, it is based on gold, similar to the current practice in mainland China. The new currency in circulation includes copper coins called "Mongo," equivalent to one copper cent in mainland China, and a denomination called "Alaba Mongo," meaning ten cents. Silver coins are called "Tegoligo" and are equivalent to one silver dollar in mainland China. There are three types of copper coins: one cent, two cents, and ten cents. There is only one type of silver coin, one dollar. There are several types of paper money, including one yuan, two yuan, three yuan, five yuan, ten yuan, one hundred yuan, fifty yuan, and ten thousand yuan. Chinese currency can also be used. Banks are located in Alata (formerly Kulun), Woodburen (formerly Chakhtu), Amaolunbate (formerly Maimachin), and other important towns.

General Customs

The customs of Inner and Outer Mongolia are the same. The clothing is still in the style of Manchu robes and jackets, wide and large, with a preference for long sleeves. However, many people now wear Western suits and leather shoes. The diet mainly consists of beef, mutton, tea, fried rice, and noodles. Although some people now eat rice, they are few in number. The cost of living in Kulun is even higher than the already high cost of living in mainland China, but in the countryside, the cost of living is extremely low. The housing consists of Northern-style houses and wooden houses in the towns, while yurts made of felt are the most common in the countryside, as they are nomadic and can be moved at any time of the year.

Opinions on Mongolia

If the central government's handling of the Inner and Outer Mongolia issue continues to follow the approach of dealing with Tibet, or sending a few special commissioners to investigate once and then considering the matter finished, I fear that failure will still be inevitable. In my opinion, the issues of Tibet and Mongolia should be approached from the perspective of the people. Within Outer Mongolia, there are already factions, and it is not too difficult to salvage the situation. If the central government does not decide on appropriate measures at this time, I fear that Inner Mongolia will also be difficult to protect in the future. The reason is that Inner and Outer Mongolia speak the same language and are of the same ethnicity. Inner Mongolia is increasingly influenced by Outer Mongolia. In the future, it is possible that Inner Mongolia will merge with Outer Mongolia or become independent on its own. Therefore, how the Mongolian issue will be resolved in the future also depends on how the central government responds.

Page 14

Respectfully submitted to the Central Party Headquarters: Previously, Wu Liande advocated opium public sales, and Li Jihong went to Taiwan to investigate the Japanese public sales methods. The Opium Prohibition and Investigation Bureau Still Open for Business Yesterday

No Instructions Received from the Opium Prohibition Committee

Several Opium Criminals Sitting and Lying Inside

Due to the enthusiastic opposition from various circles, the Executive Yuan has approved the request of the Opium Prohibition Committee to abolish the established investigation offices. Yesterday, our reporter went to the Opium Prohibition and Investigation Bureau on Xieqiao Suzhou Road and Shanghai, specifically to visit the director of the office, Feng Wenyu. Unfortunately, he was out on official business. According to the staff inside the office, the office was still open for business as usual yesterday, and the instructions from the Opium Prohibition Committee had not yet been received. The office is located at the original site of the Salt Affairs Smuggling Suppression Bureau of the Ministry of Finance, which has been painted and renovated, giving it a completely new appearance. The side rooms next to the two doors have been rebuilt into detention centers to detain captured opium criminals. The floor is covered with thick mats, which is quite clean. Yesterday, several opium criminals were lying inside.
