The Workers of the French Municipal Council Resumed Work Yesterday

Seventeen Conditions Agreed Upon

All employees and workers of the French Municipal Council went on strike to demand improved treatment. Subsequently, Mr. Du Yuesheng took on the role of mediator. For the sake of respecting the mediator's opinions, the negotiations proceeded smoothly. In particular, the workers were able to maintain order. Even during the strike period, the sanitary work was carried out as usual by Mr. Du's subordinates. Therefore, the French Municipal Council deeply understood this strike. The afternoon before yesterday, Mr. Du submitted the workers' demands to the Municipal Council, which were approved by the Council and immediately signed. Both parties were satisfied. On the workers' side, they have already resumed work yesterday afternoon. The conditions agreed upon are listed below.

Solution

The Municipal Party Committee dispatched Xu Yefu, together with Du Yuesheng, the Chinese Director of the French Concession Taxpayers' Association, to act as mediators. Regarding the issue of the treatment of all Chinese employees and workers of the French Municipal Council, a special negotiation was held at Du's residence at 12:00 PM the afternoon before yesterday. Tao Qipeng, Liu Zhigang, Wang Zhuangyong, and other members of the Employees' Negotiation Committee, and French Consul General Gangglin, the representative of the French Municipal Council, attended. After a long period of discussion, both parties agreed and signed an agreement to resolve the issue. The wages of all Chinese employees and workers will be increased by 10%. The Negotiation Committee convened a general meeting of all employees and workers at 9:00 AM yesterday, announcing that they would first symbolically resume work on the afternoon of the ninth, and fully resume work on the tenth.

Resuming Work Today

More than 5,000 employees and workers belonging to the French Municipal Council's slaughterhouse, sanitation bureau hospital, sanitation department, radio station, medical office, surveying office, accounting office, garden department, materials department, document department, printing office, engineering department, construction department, new machine room, donation office, water and electricity room, epidemic prevention vehicle, general office, astronomical observatory, comprador's office, road administration office, gravel factory, fire brigade, and other departments followed the order of the Negotiation Committee and went to their respective departments yesterday afternoon to sign in and symbolically resume work. They are scheduled to fully resume work today.

Signing of Conditions

(1) The French Concession Municipal Council agrees to allow Chinese employees and workers to establish a Chinese Employees and Workers Mutual Aid United Association. However, the rules of the association must first be approved by the Municipal Council. From the date of establishment of the United Association, the Municipal Council will provide a monthly subsidy of four hundred silver dollars and provide a suitable meeting place. (2) For the benefit of the operation of various departments of the Municipal Council, there must be a very affectionate expression between the senior and junior staff in the bureau, and there must be no unfair or malicious acts. If anyone deliberately violates the above regulations, the person in charge shall be subject to punishment. Whether the punishment is applied to European or Chinese employees, it should be resolved in accordance with the consultation of both parties by the Director of the Bureau. When the Director hears the statements of both parties regarding the causes of the disputes, a representative of the United Association may accompany the foreign party. For those who should be dismissed due to serious negligence, the Director of the Bureau should use fair and impartial means to investigate the reasons for the offense and the behavior before announcing the dismissal. (3) All long-term employees and workers of the Bureau who have served for one year can receive a year-end bonus of one month's salary. (4) For all holidays, the Municipal Council will establish a holiday list. If, due to work needs, it is necessary for some full-time employees to work on holidays, the salary that the employee should receive on that working day shall be calculated according to the following formula: (1) Sundays and holidays daily earnings = monthly salary / 30 × 2. (2) Working days calculated by the hour (divided into A and B): (A) Employees' hourly earnings = monthly salary / 30 × 6 × 2. (B) Workers' hourly earnings = monthly salary / 30 × 6 × 2. (3) Sundays and holidays calculated by the hour (divided into A and B): (A) Employees' hourly earnings = monthly salary / 30 × 6 × 2. (B) Workers' hourly earnings = monthly salary / 30 × 9 × 2. (5) The daily working hours of employees and workers remain the same, that is, employees work six hours a day, and the time may be extended to seven hours according to the needs of their respective departments, but no extra salary will be given. Workers work eight hours a day, six days a week, for a total of forty-eight hours. They have a day off on Sunday to rest. If necessary, they must continue to work during the above-mentioned time, or on Sundays and holidays, extra salary will be paid in accordance with the provisions of Article 4. (6) From July 1, 1931, all Chinese full-time employees and workers of the Bureau will receive an increase of 11% (11%) based on their current salary. (7) The Bureau will prepare a salary list for Chinese full-time employees and workers, stating the highest and lowest amounts of salary for each employee. The list will be announced on September 1 and implemented on October 1. If the current salary of old employees of the Bureau exceeds the amount specified in the list, their salary will not be reduced. However, if the salary is less than the minimum limit specified in the list, it will be increased to the minimum limit. (8) From July of this year, the salaries of Chinese employees of the Bureau will be paid in silver dollars, and one silver dollar and four dimes will be calculated as one tael of silver. (9) The Bureau will grant holidays to full-time Chinese employees in accordance with the Chinese Labor Law (Factory Law). Employees who have served for more than one year can get ten days of leave and pay their salary. (10) The Bureau will prepare a list stating the employees who are entitled to transportation allowances, and will issue them from July of this year. The allowance is six yuan per month. (11) All full-time employees of the Bureau can ask the Bureau's doctor for free consultation when they are sick, but this clause is not valid for family members. All full-time employees who want to see a doctor must obtain a consultation certificate from their superior, and hand the certificate to the doctor, who will indicate the number of sick days on the certificate and return it to the senior employee who issued the certificate, who will forward it to the Director for record. Salary will be paid as usual during the sick leave period approved by the doctor. The wages of the time of medical treatment will not be deducted for employees who have been certified by a doctor as being able to continue working. This leniency is only available once a month. If an employee is too ill to go to the doctor, the doctor will be invited to the patient's home for consultation and specify the number of holidays to be given. (12) The Savings Association for Chinese Full-time Employees of the Bureau will be established on October 1 of this year. (13) All Chinese employees who encounter danger at work shall be dealt with in accordance with the laws of the Chinese National Government (Factory Law). (14) The wages of short-term workers and coolies of the Bureau shall be the same as those stipulated by the Public Concession. The Bureau shall notify the day before if there is no need to use short-term workers the next day. (15) If this strike can be resolved peacefully, and there is no intentional damage to property, and no riotous behavior occurs against others, then all employees who participated in this strike will not be dismissed. Moreover, if the employees can resume work within 48 hours from the morning of the 8th of this month, the salary of full-time employees during the strike period will be paid as usual. (16) All the work of the Bureau's workers is assigned by the foreman, and a deadline is set. If the workers are assigned to other tasks within the specified working hours, the time will be recorded and compensated separately. (17) The Bureau will formulate a separate management regulation for Chinese full-time employees and workers. The United Association may make suggestions when formulating the above-mentioned regulations. The regulations will be implemented at the same time as the aforementioned salary list, that is, on October 1.

Statement from the Capitalists Regarding the Labor Strike at the Chinese Merchants Electric Company

Workers of the Chinese Merchants Electric Company requested the company to fulfill the labor-capital contract signed with the capitalists, so on the 4th of this month, they implemented a policy of driving the trams but not selling tickets. The Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau summoned representatives of both labor and capital to mediate. As a result, the labor side immediately restored the original state on that day. As for the requested conditions, the two issues of bonuses and housing will be resolved after the temporary board of directors is convened. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau scheduled a second conciliation committee to be convened at 8:00 a.m. today to mediate again. The previous newspaper has reported the details. It is now known that yesterday, Lu Bohong, the general manager of the company, submitted a document to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, stating: "For the purpose of clarification, your bureau's No. 11999 directive is for the purpose of replying to the previously signed labor-capital contract, proposing to add supplementary clauses, and requesting verification and approval. All submitted documents have been reviewed. After the contract has been agreed and signed, it should be followed and implemented. If there is any unclear meaning, and the two parties cannot reach an agreement, a separate request for instructions and interpretation can be submitted. If changes are made without authorization, it will only cause disputes. Please comply with this directive." After receiving this directive, the company checked the previous notification from your bureau to revise the labor-capital contract. After several conciliations, nine articles were signed on May 28 and scheduled to be implemented on June 1. The company has been implementing them in order. Now, the following will be clarified to our bureau director regarding the implementation that has been completed and can be proven: (1) Yu Ziquan, a worker in the lighting department of our company, died on June 4, and Huang Zhilan, a tea server in the transportation department, died on June 12. After being notified by the labor union, they have been handled in accordance with Article 6 of the new contract. (2) Article 3, regarding the establishment of life insurance savings, a specialist has been hired to establish a savings department on June 15 to prepare the articles of association and investigate the worker roster. The savings passbooks are being printed, so they have not been issued yet. (3) Article 5, regarding the hospital measures, St. Vincent's Hospital and Guangci Hospital have been agreed upon long ago. Representatives have been sent to the Chinese Hospital twice to discuss the subsidy funding plan, but there has been no reply. A letter was sent again on the 23rd to urge a reply, but there has been no response. Pengshoutang Pharmacy has also been contacted and agreed upon. As for Western doctor Zhu Rongsheng, he was originally the doctor appointed by the company, so there is no problem. (4) Article 7, regarding the company's one-time subsidy of 5,000 yuan and a monthly subsidy of 600 yuan from June 1, it has been stated in the agreement that the aforementioned funds will be managed and used by the Huigong (Benefiting Workers) Affairs Committee. Now that the Huigong Affairs Committee has not been established and no one is responsible for the custody, the funds have not been paid. In summary, the company has been implementing the nine articles of the contract signed with the labor union on May 28 in order. However, the board of directors believes that the last sentence of Article 2 still needs to be considered, and Article 6 must be supplemented with clauses. Therefore, they have repeatedly consulted with the labor union representatives. The representatives agreed to inform the other representatives and then reply. However, a directive from your bureau was suddenly received, based on a report from the Shanghai South District Water and Electricity Industry Labor Union, stating that the capitalists are taking the opportunity to delay. An order was issued to submit a report. The general situation has been reported to your bureau. The labor union sent a letter on the 2nd of this month, stating that the company has no sincerity in seeking labor-capital cooperation in the new contract that has been signed by both parties, and requested a detailed and accurate reply by 2:00 p.m. on July 3, otherwise the company should be responsible for any unexpected events. The company replied that the two points of amendment and supplement proposed by the company have not been answered, and the matters that should be done in the contract have already begun to draft the articles of association, but they must be approved by the board of directors before they can be implemented, and it is impossible to hold them immediately. Since it is called labor-capital cooperation, the labor side should also understand the difficulties of the capitalist side. It can be said that the company treats the labor union with sincerity. However, on the morning of the 4th, the labor union suddenly opened the trams as usual, but did not sell tickets to passengers until after 5:00, causing traffic chaos and great losses to the company. The board of directors has now decided that the workers' failure to sell tickets this time can be said to be completely unreasonable. The loss should be borne by the labor union. It is appropriate to truthfully report that the agreement has been fulfilled. Please examine and allow the labor union to be ordered to compensate the company for the loss of not selling tickets in order to uphold the rule of law and sympathize with the difficulties of businesses. As for the amount of the loss, it will be reported again after verification, combined with clarification.

The Yu Qiaqing Commemoration Ceremony is Approaching

The 50th Anniversary Celebration of Mr. Yu Qiaqing's trip to Shanghai is fast approaching. Recently, the preparatory committee has been working more intensively. For the past six months, those who entrusted Lixin Certified Public Accountants Office with matters have been handled by consultants Gu Xun, Qian Naiqi, Yu Huairen, Xu Dunqi, Wang Danru, accountants, and Zhang Qinxian, director of the Document Section. Currently, the Accounting Bureau of the National Government is in urgent need of Mr. Pan to return to preside over everything in person, so Mr. Pan submitted a request to the National Government authorities at the end of last month to resign from his various positions as Accounting Officer and Director of the Accounting Bureau. At the beginning of this month, Mr. Pan returned to Shanghai to serve the society solely as a certified public accountant and will no longer go to Beijing to hold office.

Wife Requests Declaration of Husband's Death

Sun Zhigang Has Not Returned for Ten Years

Gu Yinmei is in Dire Straits

Gu Changfa, a native of Dinghai, Zhejiang, lives at No. 1962 Yuqingli, Dongyouheng Road, is 60 years old. His daughter, Yinmei, is 33 years old and married Sun Zhigang (also known as A Gen), a native of Ningbo, in the fifth year of the Republic of China. They have two sons in total. In the tenth year of the Republic of China, Zhigang's father died of illness. Zhigang disagreed with his stepmother, Chen, and took the silver from the Shunda Clothing Store that he had opened and ran away, claiming that he was going to join the army. He never returned, and the Shunda Clothing Store was closed due to lack of a manager. Sun Chen's livelihood in Shanghai was cut off, so she returned to her hometown and abandoned Yinmei. Yinmei had no choice but to rely on her father for a living. Unfortunately, misfortunes never come singly. The two children she gave birth to died one after another. Yinmei went to work at Hecheng Tobacco Factory to make a living. For the past ten years, there has been no news of Sun Zhigang. His death is unknown. Recently, she hired lawyer Lu Qi based on Article 8 of the Civil Code, which states that after a missing person has been missing for ten years, the court may declare the person dead at the request of interested parties. She has filed a lawsuit with the Special Court, requesting that Sun Zhigang be declared dead. The petition has been delivered, but it is not known whether it will be approved. According to Shanghai's usual practice, when a husband runs away, the wife only asks for a divorce. There has never been a case of requesting a declaration of the husband's death. This case is the first case in Shanghai's personal litigation.

What Was Heard After Ye Zengshou Was Kidnapped

Father Died, Leaving a Small Inheritance

Golden Business Failed the Year Before Last

Usually Likes to Worship Buddha

Maintained Entirely by Friends

The details of the kidnapping of Ye Zengshou, manager of Zhongfu Foreign Firm, have been reported in this newspaper twice. It is now known that Zengshou's father, named Jinsheng, used to be a steward of a foreign firm. He started from scratch with diligence and thrift and was enthusiastic about charity. After Jinsheng's death, Zengshou also had his father's style, so all his friends were people of morality. He was also a devout Buddhist on weekdays, and he did his best to help whenever there was an emergency. However, he failed in the golden business the year before last, which almost led to bankruptcy. All the real estate inherited from his father was mortgaged to others. At that time, he wanted to commit suicide, but fortunately, his family noticed and was maintained by his friends, which led to this day. Even the wool textiles currently operated by Zhongfu Foreign Firm are affected by the golden business, and they are always cutting meat to mend sores, taking care of the situation. Although he had received several threatening letters from the bandits before the kidnapping, Ye Zengshou ignored them because he thought he had no savings. After the kidnapping, he did not receive any contact letters from the bandits. The Fan family and their children were extremely anxious and had no way to save him. Mei Guan'gen, the driver, was suspected by the director of the First Section of the Seventh District of being involved in Ye's kidnapping and had to be thoroughly investigated. Later, his whole family begged for bail, which shows that Ye Zengshou's usual family management is based on the principle of seeking peace and tranquility.

Gong Yan'nan, a Notorious Bandit from Nanhui, Transferred to Shanghai

The Local People Hate Him to the Bone

A Telegram Request to the Authorities to Punish Him Severely

The bandit Gong Yan'nan, also known as Xue Lan and Ye Nan, recently using the alias Shao Ruo, was born and raised in Zhujiaqiao, Nanhui, Pudong. He is a disciple of Ma Lisi, a ruthless and merciless womanizer. His wife, Lu Guifeng, is adept at aiding him in his evil deeds. He has many concubines, all of whom he plundered and later abandoned. He has a large number of disciples, such as Song Abai, Yang Qichun, Huang Yejin, Zhu Ahu, Zhou Jiannan, and hundreds of others, who serve as his henchmen. They run rampant in the villages, committing murder in broad daylight. The villagers fear him like a tiger. Anyone who dares to say a word against him is subjected to a barrage of fists. In even more severe cases, they gather a gang to retaliate and end the victim's life. As a result, the practice of armed fighting and kidnapping has become rampant in Pudong. The details of his recent arrest are as follows:

Multiple Major Crimes

Pudong has always been known for its tranquility, and the people of Nanhui are particularly honest and simple. However, since the rise of this notorious bandit and his rampaging gang, Yan Zhaoxiong, a relatively wealthy villager in the Fifth Regiment, became a target of the bandit's greed. In 1919, he was kidnapped and a huge ransom was demanded. In September 1921, a merchant named Zhang Meisong went to the bandit to collect payment for socks. The bandit chased him to the upper floor of the Zhangzhang Building and stabbed him multiple times, causing a shower of blood and instant death. In October 1927, he destroyed the Zhujiaqiao police station for gambling profits. In 1929, numerous major crimes such as kidnapping and murder occurred in the surrounding villages, including the tragic Red Disaster in Nicheng, where homes were burned and people were killed. Dozens of families, including Chu Aiqiao, Xue Haichun, Yao Huolin, Ma Qiqin, Gu Guisheng, Shi Guisheng, Gui Musheng, and Sun Changgeng, were robbed. In the Gui Musheng family, one person was even shot and killed. Zhang Zhi of Waxue Village, Yu Genlin of Yanjia Bridge, Ni Rongsheng of Tan Bridge, Jiang Zhiren of Wudian, and the son of Wang Yongqing of Chenjia Bridge were all kidnapped. The repeated incidents are too numerous to mention. All of these crimes were either personally led or instigated by the bandit leader. After the Nanhui County Government issued a warrant for his arrest, the bandit sought refuge with the lake bandit Taibao Ashu. He sent letters to merchants in Zhujiaqiao, threatening to settle accounts when the gunboats arrived. As a result, the merchants of Zhujiaqiao were constantly alarmed and unable to sleep peacefully.

Rape and Murder of a Young Girl

The notorious bandit indulged in lewd desires. He raped Bao Xiaodi's young daughter, causing her death. Other cases include the abduction of a Fengxian village girl named Adi and the daughters of villagers Wang and Zhang of Nanhui, all of whom he took as concubines and later abandoned. The villagers are all aware of these incidents.

Arrest by a Large Force

After the lake bandit leader Taibao Ashu was executed, the notorious bandit lost his patron. He then colluded with a certain Ma of the Salt Affairs Anti-Smuggling Bureau, using the alias Gong Shaoruo, and fraudulently became the captain of the Third Squadron of the Fourth Brigade of the Salt Affairs Anti-Smuggling Bureau in the Su area. He stationed his beloved disciples, Song Abai, Yang Qichun, Lu Meiting, and dozens of others, in the Nan Sitou area of Fengxian. The local area was subjected to endless harassment by them. Complaints were filed with higher authorities, but the Nanhui merchants discovered the bandit's whereabouts and requested his arrest. In April of the lunar calendar, the bandit was arrested by Brigade Commander Wu of the Fourth Anti-Smuggling Brigade. On June 3rd, the Nanhui County Government prepared a document to take custody of him, and he was finally brought to justice on the 14th.

Transferred to the Garrison Headquarters

The bandit's father, Wenbing, his wife Lu, his brother, and others, upon hearing that the bandit was being brought to justice, went around raising thousands of gold pieces to bribe officials. Recently, the Songhu Garrison Headquarters ordered the Nanhui County Government to immediately transfer the bandit Gong Yan'nan and his case file to the headquarters. After receiving the order, the Nanhui County Government compiled the case file and sent it to the headquarters. Currently, all sectors of Nanhui believe that if such a heinous criminal is not severely punished as a warning to others, the local area will be in a state of utter chaos. Therefore, they have unanimously sent a telegram requesting that he be severely punished according to the law.

Robbery of 10,000 Yuan on the Road

Four People Detained, Two Bandits Identified

Liu Caixin Has Admitted to the Robbery

Wu Heshun, a 30-year-old from Haimen, is a cook on a Taizhou steamer, frequently traveling between Hai and Shanghai. This time, when the steamer set sail from Haiqi, Wu was entrusted by Haimen Jufengzhuang Company to carry 10,000 yuan in cash to Hengfeng South Goods Store in Dasheng Lane, Xinkaihe, Shanghai, to purchase goods. Yesterday morning, the steamer arrived in Shanghai, and Wu, after tidying up, immediately divided the 10,000 yuan into two bundles of 5,000 yuan each. To be cautious, he asked his colleague Ding Awu to accompany him. At that time, it was raining heavily, so Wu wrapped the cash in oil paper to prevent moisture from penetrating. He gave one bundle to Ding, and they proceeded straight to Xinkaihe. Unexpectedly, when they reached Baodai Lane, which was close to Dasheng Lane, four robbers suddenly emerged from the roadside. One was wearing a white summer cloth gown, one was wearing a light yellow gauze shirt, and two were wearing white short outfits. They pulled out handguns, stopped Wu and Ding, and completely robbed them of the two bundles of cash totaling 10,000 yuan. As they left, they fired two shots into the ground as a warning. By the time the victims shouted for help, the robbers had already made off with the loot and disappeared into the French Concession. Wu reported the incident to the Second Precinct of the First District. Chief Yi, upon hearing the news, immediately led all the police officers to search for the robbers, but it was too late. Chief Yi urgently reported the incident to the French Police Department and, together with Chinese and foreign detectives and the two victims, Wu and Ding, conducted a door-to-door search in the inns west of Xiaodongmen. When they reached the Continental Hotel on Avenue Edward VII, they noticed a man standing at the entrance. Upon seeing the large number of detectives, he immediately looked flustered. Wu identified him as one of the robbers at the scene. He was arrested and interrogated. Three more people were arrested in a room upstairs in the Continental Hotel. Wu identified one of them. He could not mistakenly identify the other two because of their different clothing. All of them were taken into custody. After Chief Yi conducted a preliminary interrogation, the robber arrested at the entrance of the Continental Hotel confessed his name as Liu Caixin, from Ningbo, 30 years old. The other three identified themselves as Zheng Huimin, from Ningbo, 24 years old; Yang Zhurong, from Qingjiang, 38 years old; and Zhang Mingzhi, from Yangzhou, 35 years old. Their statements were extremely cunning. It is reported that the last suspect, Liu, has confessed. Zheng is also highly suspected. The other two, Yang and Zhang, are still under detailed investigation.

Zhang Fengming's Attempt to Strangle Apprentice Case

A Hearing Was Held Yesterday

Further Investigation Is Still Necessary

Qian Minglong, an apprentice at Zhang Shengji Western Clothing Store on Zhonghua Road, Xiaoximen, was sleeping soundly at dawn on the 27th of last month when he was attacked by his former colleague, Zhang Fengming, who used a trouser belt to strangle his neck in an attempt to kill him. Fortunately, he woke up early and cried for help, avoiding a fatal outcome. He immediately reported the incident to the police, who arrested Zhang and handed him over to the District Court for questioning and detention. The details were reported previously. It is now known that this case has been thoroughly investigated by Prosecutor Yang Wenjun, who has filed a public prosecution citing Article 282, Section 2 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday morning, Judge Deng Peiyi specially opened the Fifth Court and ordered the detained Zhang Fengming, 29 years old, from Ningbo, residing at 127 Bazilu, a tailor, to appear in court for questioning. Zhang stated that he worked at Zhang Shengji as a colleague in February of this year, but resigned due to slow business. He is now working at Yushunli in Dongbaoxing Road. (Judge asked) Since you have resigned, why did you come back? (Zhang answered) To find a friend. (Judge asked) When did you come? (Zhang answered) Around 11 o'clock in the evening. (Judge asked) Why didn't you go back? (Zhang answered) Because it was late and the journey back to Zhabei was far, so I borrowed a place to stay overnight at the store. (Judge asked) Do you have any grudges with Qian Minglong? (Zhang answered) No. (Judge asked) If you have no grudges, why did you want to strangle him? (Zhang answered) That's not true. I only hit him a few times with my trouser belt. (Judge asked) You confessed to strangling him at the Public Security Bureau and the Prosecutor's Office. Why are you changing your story now? (Zhang answered) I was frightened at that time, my mind was not clear, I was not in control of myself, and I said a few words in confusion. (Judge asked) How did the injuries on Qian Minglong's neck come about? Zhang was speechless. The judge ordered Qian Minglong to appear in court. He stated that he was 18 years old, from Ningbo, and an apprentice at Zhang Shengji. (Judge asked) Do you have any disagreements with Zhang Fengming? (Qian answered) No. (Judge asked) Why did he want to strangle you? According to my speculation, I am the only one guarding the store. If he killed me, he could steal the goods from the store and sell them. (Judge asked) How did he strangle you? (Qian answered) I slept in the same room with him. At around 4 o'clock, he suddenly untied my trouser belt. I was sound asleep at this time. He wrapped it around my neck and tightened it forcefully. I immediately woke up and struggled with him, crying for help. Fortunately, the tenants upstairs heard the noise and came downstairs to rescue me, so I was not strangled to death. However, I was seriously injured at the time and vomited blood, and so on. Next, the witnesses (i.e., neighbors) Mu He, Zhang Yuyuan, Yao Wang, and others testified to everything. Then, the store owner Zhang Weisheng testified that he was 56 years old, from Ningbo, and in the Western clothing business, currently residing on Avenue Joffre. He stated that he was not in the store on the night of the incident, so he did not know what happened at the time. (Judge asked) Did you dismiss the defendant because of Qian Minglong's words? (Zhang answered) I am an adult, how could I listen to the words of a child? The business was indeed slow, so I dismissed him, and so on. According to Yang Desheng, a patrol officer from the Second Precinct of the Third District, 32 years old, from Shandong, he was on duty at the Xiaoximen entrance at 3:30 that night when a child (referring to the victim Qian Minglong) ran up and claimed that he had been murdered. He listened to the statement and accompanied the child to the scene, where he saw the defendant with two trouser belts tied around his waist. He questioned him, but he was evasive and did not answer, so he took him to the police station. After hearing this, the defendant's lawyers, Xue Jiaqi and Wang Zuxun, stood up and defended the defendant. The judge stated that there was still a need to investigate this case, so he adjourned the debate and ordered the defendant to be returned to custody pending a rescheduled hearing.

The Mingyuan Lawsuit Against the Municipal Council

The English Court Declared the Case Dismissed

The Da Mei Evening News reports that after the Municipal Council ordered the Ming Shen Two Gardens to stop dog racing, the Dog Racing Association, which operates Mingyuan, sued the Chairman of the Municipal Council, Macnaghten, and the Chief Inspector, Martin, for damages of 2.5 million taels. Two Female Child Laborers Die Tragically in the Yong'an Yarn Factory

Chen Hedi and Ma Xiaohong

Both Under the Age of Fifteen

Chen Hedi, a 13-year-old female child laborer from Changzhou, living in the Yong'an Second Yarn Factory's workshop No. 41, accidentally got her clothes caught in a fine yarn machine while working in the factory's fine yarn room at around 2 p.m. yesterday. She was unable to break free, and her entire body was pulled into the roller. Her head and chest were severely injured, and she bled from the mouth. She died instantly, a tragic sight. In addition, Ma Xiaohong, a 10-year-old female child laborer from Taixing, living in Zhang Depu's contractor's residence near the factory, was hit in the head by an iron crane while working in the factory at around 4 p.m. on the same day. Her face was covered in blood. The factory immediately sent her to the Seashore Public Hospital for treatment, but her injuries were too severe to be treated, and she died soon after. Both cases have been reported by the local bailiff to the District Court for investigation.

An Ancient Elm Tree Outside the North Gate of Baoshan Was Destroyed by Lightning

There are two elm trees outside the north gate of Baoshan, on the bank of the moat. Both are more than a hug in circumference, with lush branches and leaves, providing a beautiful green shade. According to legend, they are relics from five or six hundred years ago. At around 3 p.m. yesterday, the sky was overcast with dark clouds, and there was thunder and lightning. Suddenly, there was a loud clap of thunder, and one of the trees was struck by lightning and immediately collapsed to the ground. Fortunately, it was raining heavily at the time, and pedestrians were staying indoors, so no one was injured. However, when the tree was struck and collapsed, the sky was filled with flames, and the sound shook the houses. The residents of the entire city were greatly frightened. Afterwards, the residents learned that the tree had been destroyed by lightning and rushed to watch, causing a crowded scene.

Record of Commercial Vehicle Trial Run

Contract Signed with the Railway Bureau

Contract for a Term of Five Years

Freight transportation on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou railways is congested, and there is often a shortage of vehicles. Situ Xiji gathered funds to organize the Commercial Sino-Vehicle Co., Ltd., and ordered 200 twenty-ton freight cars to help the railway bureau with transportation. The cars have now been shipped to Shanghai. Situ Xi has repeatedly discussed the terms of the lease with the railway bureau. As a result, the 200 cars ordered by the company will be supplied to the railway bureau for transportation, with a term of five years. Within five years, the company will receive one-tenth of the transportation rental fee. After five years, the vehicles will be entirely owned by the railway bureau. After mutual consultation, it was decided yesterday to transport five of the freight cars to the Rihui Port Station. Each car was temporarily loaded with ten tons of coal for a trial run to Hangzhou. If the results are stable, all of the cars can be leased.

Ye Ruchun Has Been Sentenced to Death, His Mother Requests a Retrial

Involved in the Cai Fulin Case

Whether to Grant a Retrial Has Not Yet Been Decided

Ye Ruchun, 37, from Yuyao, an employee of the Shanghai Gramophone Company on Zhifu Road, was a special police officer in the patrol. Last winter, he was suspected of being involved in the kidnapping of Cai Fulin, a comprador of the British American Tobacco Company. He was arrested by Chief Inspector Lu Liankui of the General Inspectorate and sentenced to death by the Special District Court after interrogation. Now, Ye's mother, Zhou, has hired lawyer Lu Qi to submit a petition to the Jiangsu Provincial Government requesting a retrial by the original court, listing several reasons for the request. (1) Cai Fulin identified Ye Ruchun as the driver. When Cai was at the patrol, he claimed that the driver had pockmarks on his face and spoke with a northern accent. However, in court, he saw that Ye had no pockmarks and could not speak with a northern accent, so he dropped this point. This is clearly inconsistent. (2) Cai claimed that he heard Ye's accent in the bandit's den and asked if he had blood on his head. However, Cai testified in court that there were no electric lights in the bandit's den, only kerosene lamps, so he only heard Ye's voice and could not see him clearly. However, two months passed between the time Cai was kidnapped and the time he testified in court. It is impossible to distinguish a person's voice after such a long time. This cannot be adopted. (3) Why was the photograph of the bandit leader Yang Yisheng found in Ye's home? Yang opened a toothbrush shop and was also a member of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps for more than ten years. Ye was a special police officer. It is natural for them to be friends since they were both maintaining the security of the concession. Moreover, when Ye turned 36, patrol officers, translators, and others came to celebrate his birthday and took a group photo as a memento. How can the original trial recognize this as evidence of collusion with bandits? Are all the patrol officers who were in the photo also suspected of colluding with bandits? This is unreasonable and laughable. (4) Cai's wife, Qin, testified that when contacting for the ransom, she saw Ye near Yile, as if he was keeping watch. She never testified that Ye Ruchun accompanied Rong Jian to negotiate the ransom. What Cai and Qin saw was that Qin did not go with them, and the testimony lacked the statement of being together. The original judgment was based on nothing and came out of nowhere. Why not deliberately fabricate it? The court has submitted the case file to the provincial government for review. Whether or not Ye's mother's request will be granted will be decided after a meeting of the provincial committee.

Cao Mingxi Returns from France

Cao Mingxi, a student who studied in France on a government scholarship, graduated from Shanghai Aurora University in 1925 and then went to France to study further. First, he entered the Lyon Silk Industry School for two years, and then transferred to the Paris School of Commerce to study international trade. After graduating, he interned in that country for a total of six years. He returned to China this summer and plans to use what he has learned to establish a silk factory in the Shanghai and Wuxi area to improve silk reeling methods and establish an export agency to develop foreign trade.

Will Send a Daoist Ritual for Nine Days to the Du Family Ancestral Hall

Zhang Enpu, the 63rd generation Tianshi of the Jiangxi Tianshi Mansion, also known as Ruiling, arrived in Shanghai from Jiangxi Province a week ago and stayed at the residence of a friend at No. 8 Meilan Lane, Route Lafayette, French Concession. According to reports, Zhang came to Shanghai to visit scenic spots in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. It is also known that Du Yuesheng's family ancestral hall has been completed, so Zhang will offer a Daoist ritual for nine days and a plaque. However, due to the recent hot weather, the Daoist ritual will be held when the weather cools down in the autumn.

Shanghai Has Another Female Lawyer

Ms. Shi Liang graduated from Shanghai Law College and has served in the judicial field for many years. She has successively served as an instructor in the Political Personnel Training Institute of the General Headquarters, the District Chief Training Institute of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, a standing committee member of the Jiangsu Provincial Women's Association, and the Director of Civil Training of the Qingdao Municipal Party Committee. She has profound legal knowledge and rich experience. She has now come to Shanghai and formed a partnership with Dong Kang, a senior in the judicial field, to practice law at No. 39 Avenue Edward VII.

Good News for Purchasing New-Style Residences

Meihua Company Builds Western-Style Bungalows

Exclusively for Ambitious Young People to Enjoy Happiness

Housing is the most important thing in life. In Shanghai, it is not difficult for wealthy merchants, high-ranking officials, and foreigners to own elegant and beautiful residences to suit their temperaments. However, ordinary people who serve society find it difficult to consider the quality of their housing and even more difficult to talk about buying property. Therefore, they live within their means, sharing rented accommodations. Two or three families live together in one room, separated by partitions. Not to mention the spread of diseases and the varying qualities of people, every time one is in the midst of a good dream, loud noises arise, and men and women mingle together, playing mahjong and singing loudly. Those with strong will feel the pain of insomnia, and their minds will inevitably be distracted the next day. Young people with weak will are assimilated over time and may fall into ruin. Some even find the noise of living together annoying and seek to dispel their boredom in singing halls, dance halls, pubs, and tea houses, wasting both their spirit and money. It is extremely difficult to live in Shanghai, as such. People are busy all day long, relying on their quick minds and hard work to advance society and seek personal happiness. How can it not be a great hardship if there is no suitable place to live, rest, and recuperate to adjust their bodies? In other cities in the interior, it does not take much money to find a simple and comfortable residence. However, in Shanghai, land prices have skyrocketed over the years, so how can one talk about buying property? It is now reported that the Meihua Real Estate Company in Shanghai, in view of this, has recently built forty or fifty Western-style bungalow residences on Sigao Tower Road and Xiangde Road. The architectural style is extremely new and beautiful, with gardens, open space, reception rooms, bedrooms, bathrooms, and everything else one could need. Each building is sold separately at a reasonable price. The company's purpose is to build exclusively for ambitious and moral people in society. It is still under construction and will be completed soon.

Robbery on Avenue Joffre

At around 10:20 last night, at the Nan Wansheng Cigarette Paper and Sundries Store at No. 181-183 Avenue Joffre, French Concession, operated by Shen Ruchen, a native of Ningbo, three robbers suddenly arrived. Two were wearing blue cloth jackets and trousers, and one was wearing a white short outfit and speaking with a Shandong accent. Two robbers, armed with guns, broke into the store and snatched 98 yuan in paper money, 56 yuan in silver dollars, and 180 jiao in double coins from the counter. They fled westward into Li Mei Road. The victim reported the loss to the police and requested an investigation.

Founding of the School for Specialized Language Studies

Recently, Miss Gu Shuxing, a graduate of the University of California in the United States, has, together with individuals from China, England, Germany, France, Russia, and Japan in Shanghai, established the School for Specialized Language Studies at No. 127, the intersection of Avenue Road and Xiaoshadu Road. The school teaches the languages and literature of various countries. As a specialized institution, its purpose is to cultivate translators and interpreters. The content and scale are very large, making it the pioneer of language schools in Shanghai. It is also heard that the selection of teachers is extremely strict. Instructors for each language are native speakers. Those who have already been appointed include Mr. Kirk for the German department, as well as Mrs. Hanbo, Mrs. Yu Aimili for the French department, and Miss Tuo Ge Xifa for the Russian department, all of whom have a solid foundation in literature. It is noted that Miss Gu Shuxing, after graduating from the United States, also traveled extensively to Germany, France, and Japan, specializing in language studies. She has been recommended by the initiators as the principal of the school. The board of directors includes Zhou Gengsheng, Xu Chusheng, and others.

Special Article

Abstract Translation of Feitang Report, Volume Six

(I)

Note

This article is compiled by Mr. Feitang, and is an abstract of the sixth volume of his report on the surfaces of roads outside the concessions. To see the whole picture, including charts and detailed content, one should refer to the full text of the report. The original text of Volume 3 of the report can be purchased directly from Bie Fa Foreign Firm, Sino-American Bookstore, and Evans Bookstore Limited, at the price of one dollar each. The Chinese translation is in progress.

Volume Six

This volume focuses on the surfaces of roads outside the concessions. Volume 3 of the report includes Volume 6 of the report, with a map showing the surfaces of roads outside the concessions. The so-called surfaces of roads outside the concessions are divided into two areas: one to the west of the Public Concession and one to the north of the Public Concession, surrounded by roads of the Municipal Council outside the concessions, or by the boundaries of the Municipal Council's properties connected to these roads. (1) The western area covers 7.640 acres, where Zhaofeng Park is located, divided into two parts by the arc-shaped railway tracks connecting the Jinghu and Huhang lines. (2) The northern area covers more than 283 acres, located east of the Songhu Railway line, where Hongkou Park is located.

Chapter One

This is the preface, stating that the issue of road surfaces outside the concessions is left for discussion in this volume, partly to make it clear and simple, and partly because this issue is felt to be difficult to resolve satisfactorily without reference to considerations affecting the status of the Public Concession itself. Particular attention has been paid to the extent to which the interests of residents in the Public Concession are related to the road surfaces outside the concessions. The two areas are very important to the existing Public Concession. From the perspective of future progress, their relationship is even more significant. If the Public Concession maintains its status as a great commercial and industrial center, and continues to develop accordingly, then the majority of the personnel employed by various institutions, businesses, and factories in the Public Concession will become increasingly dependent on these two areas. This is not only because the two areas can provide expanded locations for residence, but also because the land required for various activities related to the great social life and health is no longer sufficient within the existing boundaries of the Public Concession, and the two areas can meet this urgent need. Therefore, how the two areas are dealt with, and the nature of their administrative regulations, are deeply and closely related to the present and future interests of the Public Concession. (To be continued)

Youth Forum

The Summer Vacation Life of Aspiring and Energetic Youths

— Jin Peishan

Another long summer has arrived. Students, who usually live a golden university life, have returned to their hometowns to dream sweet summer night dreams. Most of the grand buildings of the universities are deserted and quiet. However, our aspiring and energetic athletes mostly come from different places in the north and south. Because the journey is long, they stay at school during both winter and summer vacations, living a different kind of holiday life. Especially the summer vacation, these two months feel like years. Now I will report on the summer vacation life of the athletes of Chih Chih University.

Xia Zeren He is the captain of the basketball team of Chih Chih University. He has worked hard for four years and won honor for his alma mater. This summer, he has earned his graduation cap and a bachelor's degree in commerce. However, he is still reluctant to leave his beloved alma mater. During the summer vacation, he gets up at 6:00 AM to practice on the basketball court. In the afternoon, he goes to the Hongkou swimming pool to swim. In the evening, he enjoys the cool breeze in Hongkou Park or on campus. The one he loves the most is his old brother Kong Guangyi. They are always together, inseparable.

Yang Linyu His hometown is far away on the Philippines Island, across the vast ocean. He hasn't been back for a long time. His summer vacation life is pleasant and healthy. He always gets up at 6:00 AM to practice sprinting, from the front gate of Chih Chih University on Jiangwan Road, back to the back gate, about a mile's distance. He does this every morning without interruption. After lunch in the afternoon, he also goes to the Hongkou swimming pool. He only returns when the sun sets and the evening breeze brings coolness. He spends every day with Zheng Mengqing, a volleyball player, because they are both overseas Chinese and speak the same language.

Xia Yushu He is Captain Xia's younger brother, nicknamed Lao San. He is famous throughout the school for his humor. Last summer vacation, at the summer school of Shanghai University, he was nicknamed the King of Humor. There are two more things that can show his humorous nature. In the scorching summer, many people are afraid of the sun and mosquitoes, so everyone cannot sleep much, and everyone's appetite must also decrease. But he still takes a nap (siesta) every day, and eats four large bowls of rice for each meal. But he has a virtue, he loves to read and study English, and is one of the best in school. He also likes to speak English, and always says "Are You Happy" when he sees people. During the summer vacation, he eats a watermelon every day. After eating, he takes another nap. His good friend is Sun Wuhou, a humorist from Soochow University. They are truly like-minded.

Kong Guangyi During the summer vacation, he not only has a ball in his hand, but also a book in his hand. It is conceivable that he likes to learn and think deeply. He likes to eat soda and ice cream, and asks the school servant to buy them every day. Because it is too hot and there are too many mosquitoes at night, he enjoys the cool breeze and does not sleep until 12:00 AM. He gets up at 6:00 AM every morning. Basketball is his specialty. Recently, because the weather has been very hot, he hasn't practiced for a long time and has been swimming instead.

Gao Dahan He is the cornerstone of Chih Chih University's soccer team. He was born in Korea. His homeland is thousands of miles away. He never returns for winter or summer vacations. He gets up at 6:00 AM every day and drinks cold water. This is truly a characteristic of Koreans. In addition to playing tennis every day, he practices Chinese calligraphy and reads new literature, especially works about love, such as "Rose Spring Dream" and "Web of Love."

Chen Bosang His home is far away in Kajang, Selangor, Nanyang. He has been studying at Chih Chih University for five years and has not returned home. He is used to school life during the summer vacation. He is a tennis player at Chih Chih University, as famous as He Zuochang. He plays tennis for more than three hours every day. Although the sun is scorching this year, it cannot stop his tennis enthusiasm. He likes to play music. He is proficient in the violin and other musical instruments. Whenever the evening breeze brings coolness and the moon is in the sky, he sings a song under the big tree on campus, which is fascinating. Sometimes, he and his Nanyang friends chat and laugh under the trees on campus, or sing "Ramona" and Nanyang folk songs. His summer vacation life has artistic interest and is very enviable.

Social News

French General Foch's Diary of the European War

— Translated by Gu Angruo

Commander Petain can restore the situation by drawing a few divisions from the reserve army and the eastern army, plus the Tenth Army and two well-trained American divisions (the Third and Fifth Divisions). However, the steps of operations on all fronts must be clearly stipulated and strictly followed. I think this is the key to turning danger into safety. On the afternoon of the 31st, I explained this point to Commander Petain and Commander Chang Xingsi (note, i.e., the commander of the Sixth Army, which was destroyed on the Ximing River) in the Curie Castle.

However, it is not enough to simply instruct the commanders to pay attention to important tasks. Now it is necessary to seek new forces to supply them. On the 31st, Commander-in-Chief Haig came to Saggs to see me. I told him that a few American divisions that are being trained in the British area may be transferred to the French side, and two divisions may be drawn from the northern detachment. When the enemy attacks the French line fiercely, the British army may need to help. Now preparations must be started.

On June 1, the enemy continued to attack without ceasing, and made major progress between the Marne River and the Ourcq River, and towards the Ferre-Cotterets Forest.

Commander Petain saw that the situation was dangerous, and emergency measures became increasingly necessary. He wrote again to inform him of the difficulties in supporting the war, and strongly requested that the American and British reinforcements go quickly.

In the letter, he attached the report of Commander Gasser, telling him that if the German army exerted pressure on the defense line of the Eastern Army, because of the lack of reserves, he would have to order a few divisions that had not been attacked to retreat quickly, and reorganize to wait for the opportunity.

This clearly shows a lack of confidence, completely disregarding the point that I specifically drew attention to in Curie Castle on May 31. In the past few weeks, I had seen the same symptoms on the British side under the same circumstances. I had to further encourage the armies.

On June 2, after a meeting with Commander Petain in Poppen, I made our conversation into the following plan and handed it to him:

"(1) The French commander must take preventing the enemy from advancing towards Paris, especially north of the Marne River, as the guiding principle of the command of the war.

"(2) On this front, we must hold on with all our strength with a step-by-step strategy.

"(3) The operating procedures of the officers and soldiers of the armies must be made into military orders, strictly followed, and any officer who is incompetent will be replaced."

In order to restore morale, I added the following clause:

"(4) All the Allied forces should do their best to help on this front."

I agreed with Commander Pershing to transfer five American divisions to the French line to take over the peaceful areas, so that the French troops in that area could be transferred to the front line to help the war. I also asked Commander-in-Chief Haig to draw three divisions from the British Army General Reserve and open them to the west of Amiens to assist the British and French armies. Finally, I moved to Morey on June 1 and to Pontpoint on June 5 in order to be close to the French General Staff.

The large French reinforcements arrived, and the front-line commanders allocated them properly. In addition, because the enemy was tired and exhausted, the situation between the Arras River and the Marne River gradually stabilized. On June 23, the German army had a difficult attack south of Soissons. On June 4, the enemy stopped attacking.

West of the Arras River, another major battle is in preparation between Noyon and Montdidier.

Commander Mangin was ordered to command this battle. On the afternoon of the 10th, I saw him in Noyon in a military hurry, and was meeting with Commander Foch on everything. He explained the battle plan to me. Although most of his teams, especially the artillery teams, could not arrive until night, he decided to launch a unified attack the next morning. He first summoned the artillery division commanders and the main army officers to give instructions on the training ground, instructing them on the opportunity to advance and assigning them combat missions. At night, the armies continued to arrive and proceeded according to the scheduled plan.

At night, Commander Mangin issued orders to the division commanders, specifying the time for the artillery to prepare and the time to carry out the attack.

(To be continued)

American International Banking Corporation at No. 17, the Bund, declares that it is registered and established by the government of Connecticut in the United States. It is organized and managed according to the highest standards of well-known savings banks in Europe and the United States, specializing in savings business. It is a pure savings bank, characterized by a permanent adherence to a sound and steady policy, guaranteeing the absolute safety of depositors' principal and interest. Therefore, the use of savings is never speculative and never engages in commercial transactions, but obtains stable income in safety, which is then distributed to depositors in fair interest. The bank is now using this idea to offer a reward for essays on the topic of "A Prudent Depositor". Entrants must use the nine advertisements published by the American International Banking Corporation in this newspaper's advertising column, such as the Chinese Bank History and the features of the American International Banking Corporation, as reference materials for their essays. The deadline for entries is July 20 for Shanghai and July 27 for other places. The judges are Fei Mengfu, Ye Kangfu, Zhang Shouqing, Zhang Shewo, and Lu Zhongyi. The first prize is 100 yuan in cash, the second prize is 50 yuan, the third prize is 30 yuan, and prizes will be given to those below the top three. The essay should be limited to 300 words and is open to all genders.
